January 1, 1940
-10,000 Japanese troops launch a counter-attack in eastern Shanxi Province in China in an attempt to relieve the nearly-surrounded Japanese 36th Division.
-<dd> 10,000 Japanese troops launch a counter-attack in eastern Shanxi Province in China in an attempt to relieve the nearly-surrounded Japanese 36th Division.</dd>
January 1, 1941
-Accounting of the previous night's bombing of London reveals that the Old Bailey, the Guildhall, and eight churches by Christopher Wren were destroyed or badly damaged. RAF bombs aircraft factories in Bremen, Germany.
-<dd> Accounting of the previous night's bombing of London reveals that the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Bailey" title="Old Bailey">Old Bailey</a>, the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Guildhall,_London" title="Guildhall, London">Guildhall</a>, and eight churches by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christopher_Wren" title="Christopher Wren">Christopher Wren</a> were destroyed or badly damaged. RAF bombs aircraft factories in Bremen, Germany.</dd>

-Twenty-six Allied countries signed the Declaration by United Nations during the Arcadia Conference.
-<dd> Twenty-six Allied countries signed the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Declaration_by_United_Nations" title="Declaration by United Nations">Declaration by United Nations</a> during the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arcadia_Conference" title="Arcadia Conference">Arcadia Conference</a>.</dd>
January 1, 1943
-German 1st Panzer Division withdraws from the Terek River area in southern Russia to prevent encirclement.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">German</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/1st_Panzer_Division_(Wehrmacht)" title="1st Panzer Division (Wehrmacht)">1st Panzer Division</a> withdraws from the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Terek_River" title="Terek River">Terek River</a> area in southern Russia to prevent encirclement.</dd>
January 1, 1945
-The Germans begin a surprise offensive (Operation Nordwind) in northern Alsace. Unternehmen Bodenplatte (Operation Baseplate) is launched by the Luftwaffe against western Allied air bases in Belgium and Holland by elements of ten different Jagdgeschwadern (fighter wings), as its last major air offensive of the war in the West. American troops kill dozens of German POWs at Chenogne
-<dd> The Germans begin a surprise offensive (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Nordwind" title="Operation Nordwind">Operation Nordwind</a>) in northern <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alsace" title="Alsace">Alsace</a>. <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Unternehmen_Bodenplatte" title="Unternehmen Bodenplatte">Unternehmen Bodenplatte (Operation Baseplate)</a> is launched by the Luftwaffe against western Allied air bases in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgium</a> and Holland by elements of ten different <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wing_(military_aviation_unit)#United_States_usage" title="Wing (military aviation unit)">Jagdgeschwadern</a> (fighter wings), as its last major air offensive of the war in the West. American troops <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chenogne_massacre" title="Chenogne massacre">kill dozens of German POWs</a> at <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chenogne,_Belgium" title="Chenogne, Belgium">Chenogne</a></dd>

January 2, 1945
-46 American B-29 bombers based near Calcutta, India attacked a railroad bridge near Bangkok, Thailand and other targets in the area. The Japanese increasingly use kamikaze tactics against the US naval forces nearby.
-<dd> 46 American <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/B-29" title="B-29">B-29</a> bombers based near Calcutta, India attacked a railroad bridge near <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bangkok" title="Bangkok">Bangkok</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a> and other targets in the area. January 10, 1941
-Lend-Lease introduced into the U.S. Congress. German–Soviet Border and Commercial Agreement is signed. German aircraft damage aircraft carrier HMS Illustrious, which is heading for Malta. German Luftwaffe, it is now clear, has command of air over the Mediterranean. The attack is also the opening of Malta's agony over the next months. Greek forces in Albania take the strategically important Klissoura pass.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lend-Lease" title="Lend-Lease">Lend-Lease</a> introduced into the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States_Congress" title="United States Congress">U.S. Congress</a>. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German%E2%80%93Soviet_Border_and_Commercial_Agreement" title="German–Soviet Border and Commercial Agreement">German–Soviet Border and Commercial Agreement</a> is signed. German aircraft damage aircraft carrier HMS <i>Illustrious</i>, which is heading for Malta. German Luftwaffe, it is now clear, has command of air over the Mediterranean. The attack is also the opening of Malta's agony over the next months. Greek forces in Albania take the strategically important Klissoura pass.</dd>

January 15, 1945
-Hitler is now firmly ensconced in the Führerbunker in Berlin with his companion Eva Braun. The British commander in Athens, General Ronald Scobie, accepts a request for a ceasefire from the Greek People's Liberation Army. This marks the end of the Dekemvriana, resulting in clear defeat for the Greek Left.
-<dd> Hitler is now firmly ensconced in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/F%C3%BChrerbunker" title="Führerbunker">Führerbunker</a> in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Berlin" title="Berlin">Berlin</a> with his companion <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eva_Braun" title="Eva Braun">Eva Braun</a>. January 17, 1941
-The Battle of Ko Chang ended in a decisive victory for the Vichy French naval forces during the Franco-Thai War.  Molotov meets German Ambassador Schulenburg in Moscow. The Soviets are surprised that they have not received any answer from Germany to their offer to join the Axis (November 26, 1940). Schulenburg replies that it has to be first discussed with Italy and Japan.

January 21, 1943
-Last airfield at Stalingrad is taken by Red Army forces, ensuring that the Luftwaffe will be unable to supply German troops any further; Hitler demands that Friedrich Paulus continue fighting and promotes Paulus to Field Marshal in order to bolster morale. Shortly after, Paulus and his forces surrender to Soviet forces, the first time a German Field Marshal is lost to surrender and thus captured by the enemy. Red Army armies have more victories in the Caucasus.

January 22, 1944
-Allies begin Operation Shingle, the landing at Anzio, Italy, commanded by American Major General John P. Lucas. The Allies hope to break the stalemate in south Italy, but they are unable to break out of the beachhead and the line holds until late May.  The minesweeper USS Portent (AM-106), commanded by Lt. H.C. Plummer, hit a mine and sank southeast of Anzio, Italy.

Lucas">John P. Lucas</a>. The Allies hope to break the stalemate in south Italy, but they are unable to break out of the beachhead and the line holds until late May. January 30, 1944
-The Japanese kill 44 suspected spies in the Homfreyganj massacre. At Anzio, Italy the disastrous Battle of Cisterna took place, as MG John P. Lucas sent Darby's Rangers to begin the breakout from the beachhead.  One of the four battalions in the action returned with only 6 of 767 men, the rest killed, wounded or captured. The Brazzaville Conference begins in French Equatorial Africa. During the conference (which lasts until 8 February), the French Committee of National Liberation (CFLN) agrees to major reforms to the French colonial empire. U.S. Navy shelling and carrier bombing began in the Marshall Islands, preliminary to invasions the following day.
-<dd> The Japanese kill 44 suspected spies in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Homfreyganj_massacre" title="Homfreyganj massacre">Homfreyganj massacre</a>. At Anzio, Italy the disastrous <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Cisterna" title="Battle of Cisterna">Battle of Cisterna</a> took place, as MG John P. Lucas sent Darby's Rangers to begin the breakout from the beachhead.  One of the four battalions in the action returned with only 6 of 767 men, the rest killed, wounded or captured. The <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brazzaville_Conference_of_1944" title="Brazzaville Conference of 1944">Brazzaville Conference</a> begins in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_Equatorial_Africa" title="French Equatorial Africa">French Equatorial Africa</a>. During the conference (which lasts until 8 February), the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_Committee_of_National_Liberation" title="French Committee of National Liberation">French Committee of National Liberation</a> (CFLN) agrees to major reforms to the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_colonial_empire" title="French colonial empire">French colonial empire</a>. U.S. Navy shelling and carrier bombing began in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marshall_Islands" title="Marshall Islands">Marshall Islands</a>, preliminary to invasions the following day.</dd>
January 30, 1945
-The Malta Conference (1945) began with Winston Churchill meeting with the Combined Chiefs of Staff on the Island of Malta in the Mediterranean to plan the end of WWII in both Theaters, and to discuss the ramifications of the Soviets now controlling most of Eastern Europe.  President Franklin D. Roosevelt would join the Conference for one day on 2 February 1945; both would fly to Yalta on 3 February for the Yalta Conference with Stalin.
-<dd> The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malta_Conference_(1945)" title="Malta Conference (1945)">Malta Conference (1945)</a> began with <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Winston_Churchill" title="Winston Churchill">Winston Churchill</a> meeting with the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Combined_Chiefs_of_Staff" title="Combined Chiefs of Staff">Combined Chiefs of Staff</a> on the Island of Malta in the Mediterranean to plan the end of WWII in both Theaters, and to discuss the ramifications of the Soviets now controlling most of Eastern Europe.  President <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Franklin_D._Roosevelt" title="Franklin D. Roosevelt">Franklin D. Roosevelt</a> would join the Conference for one day on 2 February 1945; both would fly to Yalta on 3 February for the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yalta_Conference" title="Yalta Conference">Yalta Conference</a> with Stalin.</dd>

February 2, 1943
-In the Soviet Union, the Battle of Stalingrad comes to an end with the official surrender of the German 6th Army. The German public is informed of this disaster, marking the first time the Nazi government has acknowledged a failure in the war effort. Rommel retreats farther into Tunisia, establishing his troops at the Mareth Line. Within two days, Allied troops move into Tunisia for the first time.
-<dd> In the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet Union</a>, the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Stalingrad" title="Battle of Stalingrad">Battle of Stalingrad</a> comes to an end with the official surrender of the German 6th Army. The German public is informed of this disaster, marking the first time the Nazi government has acknowledged a failure in the war effort. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Erwin_Rommel" title="Erwin Rommel">Rommel</a> retreats farther into <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tunisia" title="Tunisia">Tunisia</a>, establishing his troops at the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mareth_Line" title="Mareth Line">Mareth Line</a>. Within two days, Allied troops move into Tunisia for the first time.</dd>
February 2, 1944

Germans defeat American troops in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Cisterna" title="Battle of Cisterna">Battle of Cisterna</a> near Anzio.</dd>

February 7, 1941
-Operation Compass  After several days of desperate fighting, a flying column of XIII Corps called Combe Force cuts off the retreating Italian 10th Army during the Battle of Beda Fomm. The Italians are unable to break through the small blocking force and the British accept the surrender of roughly 130,000 Italians in and to the south of Benghazi.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Compass" title="Operation Compass">Operation Compass</a>:  After several days of desperate fighting, a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Flying_column" title="Flying column">flying column</a> of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/XIII_Corps_(United_Kingdom)" title="XIII Corps (United Kingdom)">XIII Corps</a> called <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Combe_Force" title="Combe Force">Combe Force</a> cuts off the retreating <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tenth_Army_(Italy)" title="Tenth Army (Italy)">Italian 10th Army</a> during the Battle of Beda Fomm. The Italians are unable to break through the small blocking force and the British accept the surrender of roughly 130,000 Italians in and to the south of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Benghazi" title="Benghazi">Benghazi</a>.</dd>

-Being discussed in high American government circles are plans for the internment of Japanese-Americans living generally in the western US.

February 16, 1943
-Soviet Union reconquers Kharkov, but is later driven out in the Third Battle of Kharkov. Prime Minister of Vichy France Pierre Laval and Minister of Justice Joseph Barthélemy formally create the Service du travail obligatoire (STO)
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet Union</a> reconquers <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kharkov" title="Kharkov">Kharkov</a>, but is later driven out in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Third_Battle_of_Kharkov" title="Third Battle of Kharkov">Third Battle of Kharkov</a>. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_France" title="Prime Minister of France">Prime Minister</a> of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vichy_France" title="Vichy France">Vichy France</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pierre_Laval" title="Pierre Laval">Pierre Laval</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ministry_of_Justice_(France)" title="Ministry of Justice (France)">Minister of Justice</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_Barth%C3%A9lemy" title="Joseph Barthélemy">Joseph Barthélemy</a> formally create the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Service_du_travail_obligatoire" title="Service du travail obligatoire">Service du travail obligatoire</a> (STO)</dd>
February 16, 1944
-Germans launch a major counter-attack at Anzio, threatening the American beachhead. Germans, with Panzer forces leading, fail to break out of the Korsun pocket. Diplomats from the USSR and Finland meet to sign an armistice.
-<dd> Germans launch a major counter-attack at Anzio, threatening the American beachhead. Germans, with Panzer forces leading, fail to break out of the Korsun pocket. Diplomats from the USSR and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Finland" title="Finland">Finland</a> meet to sign an armistice.</dd>
February 16, 1945
-American paratroopers and Philippine Commonwealth troops land on Corregidor Island, in Manila Bay. Once the scene of the last American resistance in early 1942, it is now the scene of Japanese resistance. American naval vessels bombard Tokyo and Yokohama.

February 18, 1943
-In a speech at the Berlin Sportpalast German propaganda minister Joseph Goebbels declares a "Total War" against the Allies; the Nazis arrest the members of the White Rose movement, an anti-Nazi youth group. Chindits under Wingate cut the railway line between Mandalay and Myitkyina.
-<dd> In a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sportpalast_speech" title="Sportpalast speech">speech at the Berlin Sportpalast</a> German propaganda minister Joseph Goebbels declares a "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Total_war" title="Total war">Total War</a>" against the Allies; the Nazis arrest the members of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/White_Rose" title="White Rose">White Rose</a> movement, an anti-Nazi youth group. Chindits under Wingate cut the railway line between <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mandalay" title="Mandalay">Mandalay</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Myitkyina" title="Myitkyina">Myitkyina</a>.</dd>
February 18, 1944
-The light cruiser HMS Penelope is torpedoed and sunk off the coast of Anzio with a loss of 415 crew. American naval air raid takes place on the Truk islands, a major Japanese naval base, but they will be one of the bypassed fortresses of the Japanese outer defence ring.
-<dd> The light cruiser <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HMS_Penelope_(97)" title="HMS Penelope (97)">HMS <i>Penelope</i></a> is torpedoed and sunk off the coast of Anzio with a loss of 415 crew. American naval air raid takes place on the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chuuk_Lagoon" title="Chuuk Lagoon">Truk islands</a>, a major Japanese naval base, but they will be one of the bypassed fortresses of the Japanese outer defence ring.</dd>

March 1, 1944

March 3, 1945
-Manila is fully liberated. Battle of Meiktila, Burma comes to an end with General Slim's troops overwhelming the Japanese; the road to Rangoon is now cleared. The Allies attempted to destroy V-2s and launching equipment near The Hague by a large-scale bombardment, but due to navigational errors the Bezuidenhout quarter was destroyed, killing 511 Dutch civilians.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Manila" title="Manila">Manila</a> is fully liberated. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Meiktila_and_Mandalay" title="Battle of Meiktila and Mandalay">Battle of Meiktila</a>, Burma comes to an end with General <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Slim,_1st_Viscount_Slim" title="William Slim, 1st Viscount Slim">Slim</a>'s troops overwhelming the Japanese; the road to Rangoon is now cleared. The Allies attempted to destroy V-2s and launching equipment near The Hague by a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bombing_of_the_Bezuidenhout" title="Bombing of the Bezuidenhout">large-scale bombardment</a>, but due to navigational errors the Bezuidenhout quarter was destroyed, killing 511 Dutch civilians.</dd>
March 4, 1941
-British commandos carry out attack on oil facilities at Narvik in Norway. British military force in Libya is thinned down as some men are sent to assist the Greeks in their emerging battle with approaching German troops. Prince Regent Paul of Yugoslavia agrees to join the Axis pact.
-<dd> British commandos carry out attack on oil facilities at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Narvik" title="Narvik">Narvik</a> in Norway. British military force in Libya is thinned down as some men are sent to assist the Greeks in their emerging battle with approaching German troops. March 6, 1944
-Wingate's Chindits make several successful forays in Burma. The Soviet Air Force bombs Narva, the city is destroyed. The Leningrad Front initiates the Narva Offensive, March 6–24. The Allies receive intelligence that the Japanese may be about to attack Western Australia, causing them to greatly bolster defenses there. When no attack comes, forces return to their regular stations on the 20th.

The Allies <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Western_Australian_emergency_of_March_1944" title="Western Australian emergency of March 1944">receive intelligence</a> that the Japanese may be about to attack <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Western_Australia" title="Western Australia">Western Australia</a>, causing them to greatly bolster defenses there. -The Secretary of War reorganizes the General Headquarters (GHQ), United States Army into three major commands - Army Ground Forces, Army Air Forces, and Services of Supply, the latter of which is later redesignated Army Service Forces. March 9, 1945
-The US firebombs Tokyo (the attack was code-named Operation Meetinghouse), with heavy civilian casualties. Amid rumours of a possible American invasion, Japanese overthrow the Vichy French Jean Decoux Government which had been operating independently as the colonial government of Vietnam they proclaim an "independent" Empire of Vietnam, with Emperor Bảo Đại as nominal ruler. Premier Trần Trọng Kim forms the first Vietnamese government.
-<dd> The US <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bombing_of_Tokyo_(10_March_1945)" title="Bombing of Tokyo (10 March 1945)">firebombs Tokyo</a> (the attack was code-named <i>Operation Meetinghouse</i>), with heavy civilian casualties. Amid rumours of a possible American invasion, Japanese overthrow the Vichy French <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jean_Decoux" title="Jean Decoux">Jean Decoux</a> Government which had been operating independently as the colonial government of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a>: they proclaim an "independent" <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Empire_of_Vietnam" title="Empire of Vietnam">Empire of Vietnam</a>, with <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Emperor_of_Vietnam" title="Emperor of Vietnam">Emperor</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/B%E1%BA%A3o_%C4%90%E1%BA%A1i" title="Bảo Đại">Bảo Đại</a> as nominal ruler. Premier <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tr%E1%BA%A7n_Tr%E1%BB%8Dng_Kim" title="Trần Trọng Kim">Trần Trọng Kim</a> forms the first Vietnamese government.</dd>

March 24, 1944
-The Fosse Ardeatine massacre in Rome, Italy. 335 Italians are killed, including 75 Jews and over 200 members of various groups in the Italian Resistance; this is a German response to a bomb blast that killed German troops. Orde Wingate is killed in a plane crash. Heavy bombings of German cities at various strategic locations last for 24 hours.
-<dd> The <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fosse_Ardeatine" title="Fosse Ardeatine">Fosse Ardeatine</a> massacre in Rome, Italy. 335 Italians are killed, including 75 Jews and over 200 members of various groups in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_Resistance" title="Italian Resistance">Italian Resistance</a>; this is a German response to a bomb blast that killed German troops. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Orde_Wingate" title="Orde Wingate">Orde Wingate</a> is killed in a plane crash. Heavy bombings of German cities at various strategic locations last for 24 hours.</dd>

March 26, 1943
-The British break through the Mareth line in southern Tunisia, threatening the whole German army. The Germans move north. Battle of the Komandorski Islands. In the Aleutian Islands United States Navy forces intercept Japanese attempting to reinforce a garrison at Kiska. Poor leadership on both sides leads to a stalemate of sorts, and the Japanese withdraw without achieving their goal.
-<dd> The British break through the Mareth line in southern Tunisia, threatening the whole German army. The Germans move north. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_the_Komandorski_Islands" title="Battle of the Komandorski Islands">Battle of the Komandorski Islands</a>. In the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aleutian_Islands" title="Aleutian Islands">Aleutian Islands</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">United States Navy</a> forces intercept Japanese attempting to reinforce a garrison at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kiska" title="Kiska">Kiska</a>. Poor leadership on both sides leads to a stalemate of sorts, and the Japanese withdraw without achieving their goal.</dd>

-On Narva front, Strachwitz Offensive destroys part of the Soviet bridgehead.

March 27, 1941
-Crown Prince Peter becomes Peter II of Yugoslavia and takes control of Yugoslavia after an army coup overthrows the pro-German government of the Prince Regent. Japanese spy Takeo Yoshikawa arrives in Honolulu, Hawaii and begins to study the United States fleet at Pearl Harbor. Hitler orders his military leaders to plan for the invasion of Yugoslavia. One result of this decision will be a critical time delay in the invasion of Soviet Union. British forces advancing from the Sudan win the decisive Battle of Keren in Eritrea. Battle of Cape Matapan the British navy meets an Italian fleet off southern Greece. The battle continues until the 29th.
-<dd> Crown Prince Peter becomes <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Peter_II_of_Yugoslavia" title="Peter II of Yugoslavia">Peter II of Yugoslavia</a> and takes control of Yugoslavia after an army coup overthrows the pro-German government of the Prince Regent. Japanese spy <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Takeo_Yoshikawa" title="Takeo Yoshikawa">Takeo Yoshikawa</a> arrives in <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Honolulu,_Hawaii" title="Honolulu, Hawaii">Honolulu, Hawaii</a> and begins to study the United States fleet at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pearl_Harbor" title="Pearl Harbor">Pearl Harbor</a>. Hitler orders his military leaders to plan for the invasion of Yugoslavia. One result of this decision will be a critical time delay in the invasion of Soviet Union. British forces advancing from the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">Sudan</a> win the decisive <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Keren" title="Battle of Keren">Battle of Keren</a> in Eritrea. Battle of Cape Matapan: the British navy meets an Italian fleet off southern Greece. The battle continues until the 29th.</dd>
March 27, 1945
-The Western Allies slow their advance and allow the Red Army to take Berlin. Argentina declares war on Germany, the last Western hemisphere country to do so; its policies for sheltering escaping Nazis are also coming under scrutiny. Argentina had not declared war before due to British wishes that Argentine shipping be neutral (and therefore Argentine foodstuffs would reach Britain unharmed), this, however, went against the plan of the USA, who applied much political pressure on Argentina.
-<dd> The Western Allies slow their advance and allow the Red Army to take Berlin. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a> declares war on Germany, the last Western hemisphere country to do so; its policies for sheltering escaping Nazis are also coming under scrutiny. Argentina had not declared war before due to British wishes that Argentine shipping be neutral (and therefore Argentine foodstuffs would reach Britain unharmed), this, however, went against the plan of the USA, who applied much political pressure on Argentina.</dd>

-The RAF sends a raid against Lübeck, destroying over 30% of the city, and 80% of the medieval centre. Hitler is outraged.

March 28, 1942
-British commandos launch Operation Chariot, a raid on the port at Saint Nazaire, France. HMS Campbeltown, filled with explosives on a time-delay fuse, rams the dock gates and commandos destroy other parts of the naval service area. The port is completely destroyed and does not resume service till 1947; however, around two-thirds of the raiding forces are lost.
-<dd> British commandos launch <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/St._Nazaire_Raid" title="St. Nazaire Raid">Operation Chariot</a>, a raid on the port at Saint Nazaire, France. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HMS_Campbeltown_(I42)" title="HMS Campbeltown (I42)">HMS <i>Campbeltown</i></a>, filled with explosives on a time-delay fuse, rams the dock gates and commandos destroy other parts of the naval service area. The port is completely destroyed and does not resume service till 1947; however, around two-thirds of the raiding forces are lost.</dd>

April 1, 1941
-British retreat after the losses at El Agheila, Libya. Rommel is surprised, then decides to continue his offensive. During this month the heavy bombing of British cities continues, and convoy losses remain heavy. In Iraq, pro-German Rashid Ali and other members of the "Golden Square" stage a military coup d'état and overthrow the regime of the pro-British Regent 'Abd al-Ilah. Rashid Ali names himself Chief of a "National Defence Government."
-<dd> British retreat after the losses at El Agheila, Libya. Rommel is surprised, then decides to continue his offensive. During this month the heavy bombing of British cities continues, and convoy losses remain heavy. In <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kingdom_of_Iraq" title="Kingdom of Iraq">Iraq</a>, pro-<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nazi_Germany" title="Nazi Germany">German</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rashid_Ali_Al-Gaylani" title="Rashid Ali Al-Gaylani">Rashid Ali</a> and other members of the "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Golden_Square_(Iraq)" title="Golden Square (Iraq)">Golden Square</a>" stage a <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Military_coup" title="Military coup">military</a> <i>coup d'état</i> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/1941_Iraqi_coup_d%27%C3%A9tat" title="1941 Iraqi coup d'état">overthrow the regime</a> of the pro-British <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Regent" title="Regent">Regent</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/%27Abd_al-Ilah" title="'Abd al-Ilah">'Abd al-Ilah</a>. Rashid Ali names himself Chief of a "National Defence Government."</dd>
April 1, 1942
-The Eastern Sea Frontier, desperately short on suitable escort vessels after the Destroyers for Bases Agreement, institutes an interim arrangement known as the "Bucket Brigaid," wherein vessels outside of protected harbors are placed in anchorages protected by netting after dark, and move only under whatever escort is available during the day. As word of this and similar measures reaches Dönitz, he does not wait to test their effectiveness, but instead shifts his U-boats to the area controlled by the Gulf Sea Frontier, where American anti-submarine measures are not as effective. As a result, in May more ships will be sunk in the Gulf, many of them off the Passes of the Mississippi, than off of the entire Eastern Seaboard.1 The Pacific War Council meets for the first time in Washington. Intended to allow the smaller powers involved in fighting the Japanese to have some input into US decisions, its purpose is soon outstripped by events, notably the collapse of the ABDA Command.2 Over 24,000 sick and starving troops (American and Filipino) are now trapped on the Bataan Peninsula.2 Japanese make landings on New Guinea, most importantly at Hollandia.3 Japanese forces begin an all-out assault on United States and Filipino troops in Bataan.3 Sustained Japanese air attacks on Mandalay in Burma.4 Germans plan "Baedeker raids" on touristy or historic British sites, in revenge for the Lübeck bombing.5 On Bataan, the Japanese overwhelm Mt. Samat, a strong point on Allied defensive line.5 The Japanese Navy attacks Colombo in Ceylon. Royal Navy heavy cruisers HMS Cornwall and HMS Dorsetshire are sunk southwest of the island.5 Adolf Hitler issues Directive No. 41, outlining his plans for the coming summer offensive in Russia. The main offensive is directed to seize the Russian oil fields in the Caucasus; a secondary thrust is to capture Stalingrad and protect the flank of the main advance.5 RAF boming raid on Cologne.6 Japanese naval forces put troops ashore on Manus Island in the Bismarck Archipelago (some sources give a date of 8 April for these landings).8 Heavy RAF bombing of Hamburg.8 American forces are strained for one last offensive on Bataan.8 With the withdrawal of HMS Penelope from Malta, Force K in Malta comes to a close.9 The Japanese Navy launches an air raid on Trincomalee in Ceylon; Royal Navy aircraft carrier HMS Hermes and Royal Australian Navy destroyer HMAS Vampire are sunk off the country's east coast.9 Bataan falls to the Japanese. The "Bataan Death March" begins, as the captives are taken off to detention camps in the north.Corregidor, in the middle of Manila Bay, remains a final point of resistance.10 Japanese land on Cebu Island, a large middle island of the Philippines.12 Japanese forces capture Migyaungye in Burma.13 Anton Schmid an Austrian soldier of the Wehrmacht is put to death, after witnessing the Ponary Massacre and saving Jews.14 Winston Churchill, concerned that the situation in Malta will cause the Axis forces in North Africa to be better supplied than British forces, sends a telegram to Sir Stafford Cripps in Cairo, asking him to pressure General Auchinleck to take offensive action before this can occur.14 USS Roper becomes the first American ship to sink a U-boat.

As word of this and similar measures reaches <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Karl_Doenitz" title="Karl Doenitz">Dönitz</a>, he does not wait to test their effectiveness, but instead shifts his U-boats to the area controlled by the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gulf_Sea_Frontier" title="Gulf Sea Frontier">Gulf Sea Frontier</a>, where American anti-submarine measures are not as effective. April 2, 1941
-After taking Agedabia, Rommel decides to take all of Libya and moves his troops toward Benghazi. All of Cyrenaic (Libya) seems ready for the taking.

April 2, 1942
-Over 24,000 sick and starving troops (American and Filipino) are now trapped on the Bataan Peninsula.2 Japanese make landings on New Guinea, most importantly at Hollandia.3 Japanese forces begin an all-out assault on United States and Filipino troops in Bataan.3 Sustained Japanese air attacks on Mandalay in Burma.4 Germans plan "Baedeker raids" on touristy or historic British sites, in revenge for the Lübeck bombing.5 On Bataan, the Japanese overwhelm Mt. Samat, a strong point on Allied defensive line.5 The Japanese Navy attacks Colombo in Ceylon. Royal Navy heavy cruisers HMS Cornwall and HMS Dorsetshire are sunk southwest of the island.5 Adolf Hitler issues Directive No. 41, outlining his plans for the coming summer offensive in Russia. The main offensive is directed to seize the Russian oil fields in the Caucasus; a secondary thrust is to capture Stalingrad and protect the flank of the main advance.5 RAF boming raid on Cologne.6 Japanese naval forces put troops ashore on Manus Island in the Bismarck Archipelago (some sources give a date of 8 April for these landings).8 Heavy RAF bombing of Hamburg.8 American forces are strained for one last offensive on Bataan.8 With the withdrawal of HMS Penelope from Malta, Force K in Malta comes to a close.9 The Japanese Navy launches an air raid on Trincomalee in Ceylon; Royal Navy aircraft carrier HMS Hermes and Royal Australian Navy destroyer HMAS Vampire are sunk off the country's east coast.9 Bataan falls to the Japanese. The "Bataan Death March" begins, as the captives are taken off to detention camps in the north.Corregidor, in the middle of Manila Bay, remains a final point of resistance.10 Japanese land on Cebu Island, a large middle island of the Philippines.12 Japanese forces capture Migyaungye in Burma.13 Anton Schmid an Austrian soldier of the Wehrmacht is put to death, after witnessing the Ponary Massacre and saving Jews.14 Winston Churchill, concerned that the situation in Malta will cause the Axis forces in North Africa to be better supplied than British forces, sends a telegram to Sir Stafford Cripps in Cairo, asking him to pressure General Auchinleck to take offensive action before this can occur.14 USS Roper becomes the first American ship to sink a U-boat.
-<dd> Over 24,000 sick and starving troops (American and Filipino) are now trapped on the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bataan_Peninsula" title="Bataan Peninsula">Bataan Peninsula</a>.<dd>2: Japanese make landings on New Guinea, most importantly at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jayapura" title="Jayapura">Hollandia</a>.</dd><dd>3: Japanese forces begin an all-out assault on United States and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Filipino</a> troops in Bataan.<dd>3: Sustained Japanese air attacks on <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mandalay" title="Mandalay">Mandalay</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Burma" title="Burma">Burma</a>.</dd></dd><dd>4: Germans plan <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Baedeker_Blitz" title="Baedeker Blitz">"Baedeker raids"</a> on touristy or historic British sites, in revenge for the Lübeck bombing.</dd><dd>5: On Bataan, the Japanese overwhelm Mt. Samat, a strong point on Allied defensive line.<dd>5: The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Imperial_Japanese_Navy" title="Imperial Japanese Navy">Japanese Navy</a> attacks <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Colombo" title="Colombo">Colombo</a> in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sri_Lanka" title="Sri Lanka">Ceylon</a>. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">Royal Navy</a> heavy <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cruisers" title="Cruisers">cruisers</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HMS_Cornwall_(56)" title="HMS Cornwall (56)">HMS <i>Cornwall</i></a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HMS_Dorsetshire_(40)" title="HMS Dorsetshire (40)">HMS <i>Dorsetshire</i></a> are sunk southwest of the island.</dd><dd>5: <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hitler" title="Hitler">Adolf Hitler</a> issues <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Case_Blue" title="Case Blue">Directive No. 41</a>, outlining his plans for the coming summer offensive in Russia. April 2, 1942
-Japanese make landings on New Guinea, most importantly at Hollandia.
-<dd> Japanese make landings on New Guinea, most importantly at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jayapura" title="Jayapura">Hollandia</a>.</dd>
April 2, 1945
-Soviets launch the Vienna Offensive against German forces in and around the Austrian capital city.  German armies are surrounded in the Ruhr Pocket.
-<dd> Soviets launch the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vienna_Offensive" title="Vienna Offensive">Vienna Offensive</a> against German forces in and around the Austrian capital city.  German armies are surrounded in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ruhr_Pocket" title="Ruhr Pocket">Ruhr Pocket</a>.</dd>
April 3, 1940
-The Ministerial Defence Committee, with the First Lord of the Admiralty (Winston Churchill) as its chair, replaces  Lord Chatfield's ministerial position of Minister for Coordination of Defence.
-<dd> The Ministerial Defence Committee, with the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Lord_of_the_Admiralty" title="First Lord of the Admiralty">First Lord of the Admiralty</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Winston_Churchill" title="Winston Churchill">Winston Churchill</a>) as its chair, replaces  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ernle_Chatfield,_1st_Baron_Chatfield" title="Ernle Chatfield, 1st Baron Chatfield">Lord Chatfield</a>'s ministerial position of <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Minister_for_Coordination_of_Defence" title="Minister for Coordination of Defence">Minister for Coordination of Defence</a>.</dd>
April 3, 1941
-A pro-Axis government is installed in Iraq. Bristol, England, suffers another heavy air attack. British troops take Asmara, the capital of Eritrea, from the Italian armies. Rommel takes Benghazi, Libya; Tobruk will remain a threat for the next seven months.
-<dd> A pro-Axis government is installed in Iraq. Bristol, England, suffers another heavy air attack. British troops take Asmara, the capital of Eritrea, from the Italian armies. Rommel takes Benghazi, Libya; Tobruk will remain a threat for the next seven months.</dd>
April 3, 1942
-Japanese forces begin an all-out assault on United States and Filipino troops in Bataan.3 Sustained Japanese air attacks on Mandalay in Burma.
-<dd> Japanese forces begin an all-out assault on United States and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Filipino</a> troops in Bataan.<dd>3: Sustained Japanese air attacks on <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mandalay" title="Mandalay">Mandalay</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Burma" title="Burma">Burma</a>.</dd></dd>
April 3, 1942
-Sustained Japanese air attacks on Mandalay in Burma.
-<dd> Sustained Japanese air attacks on <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mandalay" title="Mandalay">Mandalay</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Burma" title="Burma">Burma</a>.</dd>
April 3, 1943
-Racial tensions between American Marines and New Zealand troops of Māori origin result in the Battle of Manners Street, a small-scale riot in which no lives were lost.
-<dd> Racial tensions between American Marines and New Zealand troops of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/M%C4%81ori_people" title="Māori people">Māori</a> origin result in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Manners_Street" title="Battle of Manners Street">Battle of Manners Street</a>, a small-scale riot in which no lives were lost.</dd>
April 3, 1944
-Allied bombers hit Budapest in Hungary, now occupied by the Germans, and Bucharest in Romania, ahead of the advancing Red Army.
-<dd> Allied bombers hit <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Budapest" title="Budapest">Budapest</a> in Hungary, now occupied by the Germans, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bucharest" title="Bucharest">Bucharest</a> in Romania, ahead of the advancing Red Army.</dd>
April 4, 1941
-Rommel is now about 200 miles east of El Agheila, heading for Tobruk and Egypt. An Atlantic convoy suffers almost 50% losses to U-boat campaign.
-<dd> Rommel is now about 200 miles east of El Agheila, heading for Tobruk and Egypt. An Atlantic convoy suffers almost 50% losses to U-boat campaign.</dd>
April 4, 1942
-Germans plan "Baedeker raids" on touristy or historic British sites, in revenge for the Lübeck bombing.
-<dd> Germans plan <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Baedeker_Blitz" title="Baedeker Blitz">"Baedeker raids"</a> on touristy or historic British sites, in revenge for the Lübeck bombing.</dd>
April 4, 1943
-The only large-scale escape of Allied prisoners-of-war from the Japanese in the Pacific takes place when ten American POWs and two Filipino convicts break out of the Davao Penal Colony on the island of Mindanao in the southern Philippines. The escaped POWs were the first to break the news of the infamous Bataan Death March and other atrocities committed by the Japanese to the world.
-<dd> The only large-scale escape of Allied prisoners-of-war from the Japanese in the Pacific takes place when ten American POWs and two Filipino convicts break out of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Davao_Penal_Colony" title="Davao Penal Colony">Davao Penal Colony</a> on the island of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mindanao" title="Mindanao">Mindanao</a> in the southern Philippines. The escaped POWs were the first to break the news of the infamous <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bataan_Death_March" title="Bataan Death March">Bataan Death March</a> and other atrocities committed by the Japanese to the world.</dd>
April 4, 1944
-General Charles de Gaulle takes command of all Free French forces.
-<dd> General <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charles_de_Gaulle" title="Charles de Gaulle">Charles de Gaulle</a> takes command of all Free French forces.</dd>
April 4, 1945
-Bratislava, the capital of the Slovak Republic, is overrun by advancing Soviet forces. The remaining members of President Jozef Tiso's pro-German government flee to Austria. The Ohrdruf death camp is liberated by the Allies.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bratislava" title="Bratislava">Bratislava</a>, the capital of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_Republic_(1939-1945)" title="Slovak Republic (1939-1945)">Slovak Republic</a>, is overrun by advancing Soviet forces. The remaining members of President <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jozef_Tiso" title="Jozef Tiso">Jozef Tiso</a>'s pro-German government flee to Austria. The <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ohrdruf_death_camp" title="Ohrdruf death camp">Ohrdruf death camp</a> is liberated by the Allies.</dd>
April 5, 1942
-On Bataan, the Japanese overwhelm Mt. Samat, a strong point on Allied defensive line.5 The Japanese Navy attacks Colombo in Ceylon. Royal Navy heavy cruisers HMS Cornwall and HMS Dorsetshire are sunk southwest of the island.5 Adolf Hitler issues Directive No. 41, outlining his plans for the coming summer offensive in Russia. The main offensive is directed to seize the Russian oil fields in the Caucasus; a secondary thrust is to capture Stalingrad and protect the flank of the main advance.5 RAF boming raid on Cologne.6 Japanese naval forces put troops ashore on Manus Island in the Bismarck Archipelago (some sources give a date of 8 April for these landings).8 Heavy RAF bombing of Hamburg.8 American forces are strained for one last offensive on Bataan.8 With the withdrawal of HMS Penelope from Malta, Force K in Malta comes to a close.9 The Japanese Navy launches an air raid on Trincomalee in Ceylon; Royal Navy aircraft carrier HMS Hermes and Royal Australian Navy destroyer HMAS Vampire are sunk off the country's east coast.9 Bataan falls to the Japanese. The "Bataan Death March" begins, as the captives are taken off to detention camps in the north.Corregidor, in the middle of Manila Bay, remains a final point of resistance.
-<dd> On Bataan, the Japanese overwhelm Mt. Samat, a strong point on Allied defensive line.<dd>5: The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Imperial_Japanese_Navy" title="Imperial Japanese Navy">Japanese Navy</a> attacks <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Colombo" title="Colombo">Colombo</a> in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sri_Lanka" title="Sri Lanka">Ceylon</a>. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">Royal Navy</a> heavy <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cruisers" title="Cruisers">cruisers</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HMS_Cornwall_(56)" title="HMS Cornwall (56)">HMS <i>Cornwall</i></a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HMS_Dorsetshire_(40)" title="HMS Dorsetshire (40)">HMS <i>Dorsetshire</i></a> are sunk southwest of the island.</dd><dd>5: <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hitler" title="Hitler">Adolf Hitler</a> issues <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Case_Blue" title="Case Blue">Directive No. 41</a>, outlining his plans for the coming summer offensive in Russia. The main offensive is directed to seize the Russian oil fields in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caucasus" title="Caucasus">Caucasus</a>; a secondary thrust is to capture <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stalingrad" title="Stalingrad">Stalingrad</a> and protect the flank of the main advance.</dd><dd>5: <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/RAF" title="RAF">RAF</a> boming raid on Cologne.</dd><dd>6: Japanese naval forces put troops ashore on <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Manus_Island" title="Manus Island">Manus Island</a> in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bismarck_Archipelago" title="Bismarck Archipelago">Bismarck Archipelago</a> (some sources give a date of 8 April for these landings).</dd><dd>8: Heavy RAF bombing of Hamburg.</dd><dd>8: American forces are strained for one last offensive on Bataan.</dd><dd>8: With the withdrawal of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HMS_Penelope_(97)" title="HMS Penelope (97)">HMS <i>Penelope</i></a> from Malta, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Force_K" title="Force K">Force K</a> in Malta comes to a close.</dd><dd>9: The Japanese Navy launches an air raid on <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Trincomalee" title="Trincomalee">Trincomalee</a> in Ceylon; Royal Navy <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aircraft_carrier" title="Aircraft carrier">aircraft carrier</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HMS_Hermes_(95)" title="HMS Hermes (95)">HMS <i>Hermes</i></a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Royal_Australian_Navy" title="Royal Australian Navy">Royal Australian Navy</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Destroyer" title="Destroyer">destroyer</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HMAS_Vampire_(D68)" title="HMAS Vampire (D68)">HMAS <i>Vampire</i></a> are sunk off the country's east coast.</dd><dd>9: Bataan falls to the Japanese. The "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bataan_Death_March" title="Bataan Death March">Bataan Death March</a>" begins, as the captives are taken off to detention camps in the north.</dd>Corregidor, in the middle of Manila Bay, remains a final point of resistance.</dd>
April 5, 1942
-The Japanese Navy attacks Colombo in Ceylon. Royal Navy heavy cruisers HMS Cornwall and HMS Dorsetshire are sunk southwest of the island.
-<dd> The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Imperial_Japanese_Navy" title="Imperial Japanese Navy">Japanese Navy</a> attacks <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Colombo" title="Colombo">Colombo</a> in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sri_Lanka" title="Sri Lanka">Ceylon</a>. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">Royal Navy</a> heavy <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cruisers" title="Cruisers">cruisers</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HMS_Cornwall_(56)" title="HMS Cornwall (56)">HMS <i>Cornwall</i></a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HMS_Dorsetshire_(40)" title="HMS Dorsetshire (40)">HMS <i>Dorsetshire</i></a> are sunk southwest of the island.</dd>
April 5, 1942
-Adolf Hitler issues Directive No. 41, outlining his plans for the coming summer offensive in Russia. The main offensive is directed to seize the Russian oil fields in the Caucasus; a secondary thrust is to capture Stalingrad and protect the flank of the main advance.
-<dd> <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hitler" title="Hitler">Adolf Hitler</a> issues <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Case_Blue" title="Case Blue">Directive No. 41</a>, outlining his plans for the coming summer offensive in Russia. The main offensive is directed to seize the Russian oil fields in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Caucasus" title="Caucasus">Caucasus</a>; a secondary thrust is to capture <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stalingrad" title="Stalingrad">Stalingrad</a> and protect the flank of the main advance.</dd>
April 5, 1942
-RAF boming raid on Cologne.
-<dd> <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/RAF" title="RAF">RAF</a> boming raid on Cologne.</dd>
April 5, 1944
-US Air Force bombs Ploesti oil fields in Romania, with heavy losses.
-<dd> US Air Force bombs Ploesti oil fields in Romania, with heavy losses.</dd>
April 6, 1941
-Forces of Germany, Hungary, and Italy, moving through Romania and Hungary, initiate the invasions of Yugoslavia and Greece. The Italian Army is driven out from Addis Ababa, Ethiopia. The northern wing of Rommel's forces take Derna, on the Libyan coast. The southern wing moves toward Mechili, and takes it on the 8th.
-<dd> Forces of Germany, Hungary, and Italy, moving through Romania and Hungary, initiate the invasions of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Invasion_of_Yugoslavia" title="Invasion of Yugoslavia">Yugoslavia</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Greece" title="Battle of Greece">Greece</a>. The Italian Army is driven out from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Addis_Ababa" title="Addis Ababa">Addis Ababa</a>, Ethiopia. The northern wing of Rommel's forces take Derna, on the Libyan coast. The southern wing moves toward <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mechili" title="Mechili">Mechili</a>, and takes it on the 8th.</dd>
April 6, 1942
-Japanese naval forces put troops ashore on Manus Island in the Bismarck Archipelago (some sources give a date of 8 April for these landings).
-<dd> Japanese naval forces put troops ashore on <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Manus_Island" title="Manus Island">Manus Island</a> in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bismarck_Archipelago" title="Bismarck Archipelago">Bismarck Archipelago</a> (some sources give a date of 8 April for these landings).</dd>
April 6, 1944
-The Japanese drive on the Plain of Imphal, supposedly halted, proves strong enough to surround British forces at Imphal and Kohima, in India.
-<dd> The Japanese drive on the Plain of Imphal, supposedly halted, proves strong enough to surround British forces at Imphal and Kohima, in India.</dd>
April 6, 1945
-The Spring 1945 offensive in Italy begins in northern Italy.
-<dd> The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spring_1945_offensive_in_Italy" title="Spring 1945 offensive in Italy">Spring 1945 offensive in Italy</a> begins in northern Italy.</dd>
April 7, 1941
-The Luftwaffe begins a two-day assault on Belgrade, Yugoslavia; Hitler is infuriated by the Yugoslav resistance.
-<dd> The Luftwaffe begins a two-day assault on Belgrade, Yugoslavia; Hitler is infuriated by the Yugoslav resistance.</dd>
April 7, 1943
-Hitler and Mussolini come together at Salzburg, mostly for the purpose of propping up Mussolini's fading morale. Allied forces–the Americans from the West, the British from the East–link up near Gafsa in Tunisia. Bolivia declares war on Germany, Japan, and Italy.
-<dd> Hitler and Mussolini come together at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Salzburg" title="Salzburg">Salzburg</a>, mostly for the purpose of propping up Mussolini's fading morale. Allied forces–the Americans from the West, the British from the East–link up near Gafsa in Tunisia. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bolivia" title="Bolivia">Bolivia</a> declares war on Germany, Japan, and Italy.</dd>
April 7, 1945
-The Japanese battleship Yamato is sunk in the waters north of Okinawa as the Japanese make their last major naval operation.
-<dd> The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_battleship_Yamato" title="Japanese battleship Yamato">Japanese battleship <i>Yamato</i></a> is sunk in the waters north of <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Okinawa" title="Okinawa">Okinawa</a> as the Japanese make their <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Ten-Go" title="Operation Ten-Go">last major naval operation</a>.</dd>
April 8, 1941
-The Germans take Salonika, Greece.
-<dd> The Germans take Salonika, Greece.</dd>
April 8, 1942
-Heavy RAF bombing of Hamburg.
-<dd> Heavy RAF bombing of Hamburg.</dd>
April 8, 1942
-American forces are strained for one last offensive on Bataan.
-<dd> American forces are strained for one last offensive on Bataan.</dd>
April 8, 1942
-With the withdrawal of HMS Penelope from Malta, Force K in Malta comes to a close.
-<dd> With the withdrawal of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HMS_Penelope_(97)" title="HMS Penelope (97)">HMS <i>Penelope</i></a> from Malta, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Force_K" title="Force K">Force K</a> in Malta comes to a close.</dd>
April 8, 1944
-The Red Army attacks in an attempt to retake all of the Crimea, the Germans retreat westward to Sevastopol.
-<dd> The Red Army attacks in an attempt to retake all of the Crimea, the Germans retreat westward to Sevastopol.</dd>
April 9, 1940
-Germans land in several Norwegian ports and take Oslo; the Norwegian Campaign lasts two months. The British start their Norwegian Campaign. Denmark is invaded and surrenders in six hours. The German heavy cruiser Blücher is sunk at the Battle of Drøbak Sound.
-<dd> Germans land in several Norwegian ports and take <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oslo" title="Oslo">Oslo</a>; the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_Campaign" title="Norwegian Campaign">Norwegian Campaign</a> lasts two months. The British start their Norwegian Campaign. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_invasion_of_Denmark_(1940)" title="German invasion of Denmark (1940)">Denmark is invaded</a> and surrenders in six hours. The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_cruiser_Bl%C3%BCcher" title="German cruiser Blücher">German heavy cruiser Blücher</a> is sunk at the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Dr%C3%B8bak_Sound" title="Battle of Drøbak Sound">Battle of Drøbak Sound</a>.</dd>
April 9, 1942
-The Japanese Navy launches an air raid on Trincomalee in Ceylon; Royal Navy aircraft carrier HMS Hermes and Royal Australian Navy destroyer HMAS Vampire are sunk off the country's east coast.
-<dd> The Japanese Navy launches an air raid on <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Trincomalee" title="Trincomalee">Trincomalee</a> in Ceylon; Royal Navy <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aircraft_carrier" title="Aircraft carrier">aircraft carrier</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HMS_Hermes_(95)" title="HMS Hermes (95)">HMS <i>Hermes</i></a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Royal_Australian_Navy" title="Royal Australian Navy">Royal Australian Navy</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Destroyer" title="Destroyer">destroyer</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HMAS_Vampire_(D68)" title="HMAS Vampire (D68)">HMAS <i>Vampire</i></a> are sunk off the country's east coast.</dd>

-Bataan falls to the Japanese. The "Bataan Death March" begins, as the captives are taken off to detention camps in the north.

April 9, 1945
-The Battle of Königsberg ends in a Soviet victory. A heavy bombing at Kiel by the RAF destroys the last two major German warships, the heavy cruisers Admiral Hipper and Admiral Scheer. Pastor Dietrich Bonhoeffer is executed at Flossenburg prison.
-<dd> The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_K%C3%B6nigsberg" title="Battle of Königsberg">Battle of Königsberg</a> ends in a Soviet victory. A heavy bombing at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kiel" title="Kiel">Kiel</a> by the RAF destroys the last two major German warships, the heavy cruisers <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_cruiser_Admiral_Hipper" title="German cruiser Admiral Hipper"><i>Admiral Hipper</i></a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_cruiser_Admiral_Scheer" title="German cruiser Admiral Scheer"><i>Admiral Scheer</i></a>. Pastor <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dietrich_Bonhoeffer" title="Dietrich Bonhoeffer">Dietrich Bonhoeffer</a> is executed at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Flossenb%C3%BCrg_concentration_camp" title="Flossenbürg concentration camp">Flossenburg</a> prison.</dd>
April 10, 1940
-Germans set up a Norwegian government under Vidkun Quisling, former minister of defence. The German light cruiser Königsberg is sunk by British Fleet Air Arm dive bombers.

April 10, 1941
-Greenland is occupied by the United States. With the approval of a "free Denmark", the US will build naval and air bases as counters to the U-boat war. While still being invaded, the Kingdom of Yugoslavia is split up by Germany and Italy. The Independent State of Croatia (Nezavisna Država Hrvatska, NDH) is established under Ante Pavelić and his Ustaša. Germans encircle the port of Tobruk, Libya, opening the siege; some of Rommel's forces move east to take Fort Capuzzo and Sollum, on the border with Egypt. The destroyer USS Niblack attacks a German U-boat that had just sunk a Dutch freighter. The Niblack was picking up survivors of the freighter when it detected the U-boat preparing to attack. The Niblack attacked with depth charges and drove off the U-boat.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greenland" title="Greenland">Greenland</a> is occupied by the United States. With the approval of a "free Denmark", the US will build naval and air bases as counters to the U-boat war. While still being invaded, the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kingdom_of_Yugoslavia" title="Kingdom of Yugoslavia">Kingdom of Yugoslavia</a> is split up by Germany and Italy. The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Independent_State_of_Croatia" title="Independent State of Croatia">Independent State of Croatia</a> (Nezavisna Država Hrvatska, NDH) is established under <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ante_Paveli%C4%87" title="Ante Pavelić">Ante Pavelić</a> and his <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Usta%C5%A1a" title="Ustaša">Ustaša</a>. Germans encircle the port of Tobruk, Libya, opening the siege; some of Rommel's forces move east to take Fort Capuzzo and Sollum, on the border with Egypt. The destroyer <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/USS_Niblack_(DD-424)" title="USS Niblack (DD-424)">USS <i>Niblack</i></a> attacks a German U-boat that had just sunk a Dutch freighter. The <i>Niblack</i> was picking up survivors of the freighter when it detected the U-boat preparing to attack. The <i>Niblack</i> <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_American_shots_fired_in_World_War_II" title="First American shots fired in World War II">attacked with depth charges and drove off the U-boat</a>.</dd>

April 13, 1945
-The Vienna Offensive ends with a Soviet victory.  Gardelegen Massacre takes place. Over 1000 slave laborers were closed in a barn which then was set on fire. It was one of the last massacres on civil population perpetrated by Germans. Just few hours later, American troops captured Gardelegen
-<dd> The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vienna_Offensive" title="Vienna Offensive">Vienna Offensive</a> ends with a Soviet victory.  <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gardelegen_Massacre" title="Gardelegen Massacre">Gardelegen Massacre</a> takes place. Over 1000 slave laborers were closed in a barn which then was set on fire. It was one of the last massacres on civil population perpetrated by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germans" title="Germans">Germans</a>. Just few hours later, American troops captured <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gardelegen" title="Gardelegen">Gardelegen</a></dd>

April 14, 1941

April 18, 1942

This deprives U-boat commanders of background illumination, but provides only a very little relief from U-boat attack; as the nights grow shorter more U-boat attacks are occurring in daylight hours.

April 18, 1943
-Admiral Isoroku Yamamoto, chief architect of Japanese naval strategy, is killed when his plane is shot down by American P38's over Bougainville. He was on an inspection tour. The "Palm Sunday massacre" large numbers of German troop-transport aircraft are shot down before reaching Tunisia, where they were to pick up the isolated German troops.
-<dd> Admiral <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isoroku_Yamamoto" title="Isoroku Yamamoto">Isoroku Yamamoto</a>, chief architect of Japanese naval strategy, is killed when his plane is shot down by American <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lockheed_P-38_Lightning" title="Lockheed P-38 Lightning">P38's</a> over Bougainville. He was on an inspection tour. The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Flax" title="Operation Flax">"Palm Sunday massacre"</a>: large numbers of German troop-transport aircraft are shot down before reaching Tunisia, where they were to pick up the isolated German troops.</dd>

April 20, 1942
-General Dobbie, Governor-General and Commander-in-Chief of Malta, sends a message to Winston Churchill saying "it is obvious that the very worst may happen if we cannot replenish our vital needs, especially flour and ammunition, and that very soon...." Churchill concludes from this and other "disturbing news" that Dobbie is not capable enough for such an important job, and decides to replace him with Lord Gort.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Dobbie" title="William Dobbie">General Dobbie</a>, Governor-General and Commander-in-Chief of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malta" title="Malta">Malta</a>, sends a message to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Winston_Churchill" title="Winston Churchill">Winston Churchill</a> saying "it is obvious that the very worst may happen if we cannot replenish our vital needs, especially flour and ammunition, and that very soon...." Churchill concludes from this and other "disturbing news" that Dobbie is not capable enough for such an important job, and decides to replace him with <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lord_Gort" title="Lord Gort">Lord Gort</a>.</dd>

April 22, 1945
-Hitler is informed late in the day that, with the approval of Gotthard Heinrici, Steiner's attack was never launched. Instead, Steiner's forces were authorised to retreat. In response, Hitler launches a furious tirade against the perceived treachery and incompetence of his military commanders in front of Wilhelm Keitel, Hans Krebs, Alfred Jodl, Wilhelm Burgdorf and Martin Bormann. Hitler's tirade culminates in an oath to stay in Berlin to head up the defence of the city. Hitler orders General Walther Wenck to attack towards Berlin with the Twelfth Army, link up with the Ninth Army of General Theodor Busse, and relieve the city.  Wenck launched an attack, but it will come to nothing.
-<dd> Hitler is informed late in the day that, with the approval of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gotthard_Heinrici" title="Gotthard Heinrici">Gotthard Heinrici</a>, Steiner's attack was never launched. Instead, Steiner's forces were authorised to retreat. In response, Hitler launches a furious tirade against the perceived treachery and incompetence of his military commanders in front of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wilhelm_Keitel" title="Wilhelm Keitel">Wilhelm Keitel</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hans_Krebs_(Wehrmacht_general)" title="Hans Krebs (Wehrmacht general)">Hans Krebs</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alfred_Jodl" title="Alfred Jodl">Alfred Jodl</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wilhelm_Burgdorf" title="Wilhelm Burgdorf">Wilhelm Burgdorf</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Martin_Bormann" title="Martin Bormann">Martin Bormann</a>. April 23, 1945
-Hermann Göring sends a radiogram to Hitler's bunker, asking to be declared Hitler's successor. He proclaims that if he gets no response by 10 PM, he will assume Hitler is incapacitated and assume leadership of the Reich. Furious, Hitler strips him of all his offices and expels him from the Nazi Party. Albert Speer makes one last visit to Hitler, informing him that he (Speer) ignored the Nero Decree for scorched earth.

Furious, Hitler strips him of all his offices and expels him from the Nazi Party. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albert_Speer" title="Albert Speer">Albert Speer</a> makes one last visit to Hitler, informing him that he (Speer) ignored the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nero_Decree" title="Nero Decree">Nero Decree</a> for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scorched_earth" title="Scorched earth">scorched earth</a>.</dd>

April 24, 1945
-Himmler, ignoring the orders of Hitler, makes a secret surrender offer to the Allies, (led by Count Folke Bernadotte, head of the Red Cross), provided that the Red Army is not involved. The offer is rejected; when Hitler hears of the betrayal on the 28th, he orders Himmler shot. Forces of the 1st Belorussian Front and the 1st Ukrainian Front link up in the initial encirclement of Berlin. Allies encircle the last German armies near Bologna, and the Italian war in effect comes to an end.
-<dd> Himmler, ignoring the orders of Hitler, makes a secret surrender offer to the Allies, (led by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Folke_Bernadotte" title="Folke Bernadotte">Count Folke Bernadotte</a>, head of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Red_Cross_and_Red_Crescent_Movement" title="International Red Cross and Red Crescent Movement">Red Cross</a>), provided that the Red Army is not involved. The offer is rejected; when Hitler hears of the betrayal on the 28th, he orders Himmler shot. Forces of the 1st Belorussian Front and the 1st Ukrainian Front link up in the initial encirclement of Berlin. Allies encircle the last German armies near <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bologna" title="Bologna">Bologna</a>, and the Italian war in effect comes to an end.</dd>

April 28, 1945
-Mussolini and his mistress Clara Petacci, are shot, and hanged by the feet upside down in Milan.  Other members of his puppet government are also executed by Italian partisans and their bodies put on display.28 The 148th German Division surrender to Brazilian Expeditionary Division.29 Dachau concentration camp is liberated by the U.S. 7th Army. All forces in Italy officially surrender and a ceasefire is declared. Allied air forces commence Operations Manna and Chowhound, providing food aid to the Netherlands under a truce made with occupying German forces. Hitler marries his companion Eva Braun.30 Hitler and his wife commit suicide with a combination of poison and a gunshot. Before he dies, he dictates his last will and testament. In it Joseph Goebbels is appointed Reich Chancellor and Grand Admiral Karl Dönitz is appointed Reich President.

April 29, 1942
-Adolf Hitler summons Benito Mussolini and Galeazzo Ciano to a summit conference at Salzburg. Like most Hitlerian conferences, this one is actually a thinly-disguised attempt to harangue the invitees into compliance with the Fuehrer's will; in this case, the Italians are to commit more troops to the Eastern Front. Hitler is successful, and Mussolini agrees to send an additional seven divisions, as well as the two already promised. These unfortunate troops will be formed into the Eighth Italian Army and attached to von Bock's (later von Weichs's) Army Group B.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Adolf_Hitler" title="Adolf Hitler">Adolf Hitler</a> summons <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Benito_Mussolini" title="Benito Mussolini">Benito Mussolini</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Galeazzo_Ciano" title="Galeazzo Ciano">Galeazzo Ciano</a> to a summit conference at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Salzburg" title="Salzburg">Salzburg</a>. Like most Hitlerian conferences, this one is actually a thinly-disguised attempt to harangue the invitees into compliance with the Fuehrer's will; in this case, the Italians are to commit more troops to the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eastern_Front_(World_War_II)" title="Eastern Front (World War II)">Eastern Front</a>. Hitler is successful, and Mussolini agrees to send an additional seven divisions, as well as the two already promised. These unfortunate troops will be formed into the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_Army_in_Russia" title="Italian Army in Russia">Eighth Italian Army</a> and attached to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fedor_von_Bock" title="Fedor von Bock">von Bock's</a> (later <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maximilian_von_Weichs" title="Maximilian von Weichs">von Weichs's</a>) <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Army_Group_B" title="Army Group B">Army Group B</a>.</dd>

May 1, 1941

May 1, 1942
-Rommel readies for a new offensive during the early part of this month.1 Troops of the Japanese Fifteenth Army under General Shojiro Iida take Mandalay and Monywa, securing the western terminus of the Burma Road.2 In response to American intelligence intercepts, which warn of the impending Japanese landings, the Australian garrison is evacuated from Tulagi.3 In the initial move of the Japanese strategic plan to capture Port Moresby, Japanese forces under Admiral Kiyohide Shima make unopposed landings on Tulagi, opening the Battle of the Coral Sea.3 American General Joseph Stilwell decides that nothing more can be accomplished in Burma, and that the time has come to evacuate.4 US Rear Admiral Frank Jack Fletcher's Task Force 17 makes the first carrier strike of the Battle of the Coral Sea, attacking Japanese naval targets near Tulagi.4 Howell and his party of 114, mostly Americans, begin their trek to the Indian border and safety. To reach India, Stilwell will not only have to stay ahead of the Japanese, but beat the coming monsoon.5 Heavy Japanese artillery attack on Corregidor.5 British forces begin "Operation Ironclad" the invasion of Madagascar to keep the Vichy French territory from falling to a possible Japanese invasion.5 The city of Exeter is bombed by the Luftwaffe, another "Baedeker Raid".5 In the Coral Sea, both Japanese and American carrier aircraft spend this day and the following one searching for each other's ships, with no success, even though at one point the opposing carrier groups are separated by less than a hundred miles of ocean.6 General Stilwell abandons his trucks, which constantly become stuck and so are actually impeding progress rather than aiding it. He retains his Jeeps, which do better. Late in the day his party arrives at Indaw.
-<dd> Rommel readies for a new offensive during the early part of this month.<dd>1: Troops of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_Fifteenth_Army" title="Japanese -Troops of the Japanese Fifteenth Army under General Shojiro Iida take Mandalay and Monywa, securing the western terminus of the Burma Road.

May 1, 1945
-German General Hans Krebs negotiates the surrender of the city of Berlin with Soviet General Vasily Chuikov. Chuikov, as commander of the Soviet 8th Guards Army, commands the Soviet forces in central Berlin. Krebs is not authorized by Reich Chancellor Goebbels to agree to an unconditional surrender, so his negotiations with Chuikov end with no agreement. Goebbels and his wife murder their children and commit suicide. Yugoslavian Partisan leader Josip Broz Tito and his troops capture Trieste, Italy. New Zealand troops play a supporting role. The war in Italy is over but some German troops are still not accounted for. Australian troops land on Tarakan island off the coast of Borneo
-<dd> German General <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hans_Krebs_(Wehrmacht_general)" title="Hans Krebs (Wehrmacht general)">Hans Krebs</a> negotiates the surrender of the city of Berlin with Soviet General <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vasily_Chuikov" title="Vasily Chuikov">Vasily Chuikov</a>. Chuikov, as commander of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Soviet_8th_Guards_Army" title="Soviet 8th Guards Army">Soviet 8th Guards Army</a>, commands the Soviet forces in central Berlin. Krebs is not authorized by Reich Chancellor Goebbels to agree to an unconditional surrender, so his negotiations with Chuikov end with no agreement. Goebbels and his wife murder <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Goebbels_children" title="Goebbels children">their children</a> and commit suicide. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yugoslavia" title="Yugoslavia">Yugoslavian</a> Partisan leader <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Josip_Broz_Tito" title="Josip Broz Tito">Josip Broz Tito</a> and his troops capture <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Trieste" title="Trieste">Trieste</a>, Italy. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Zealand" title="New Zealand">New Zealand</a> troops play a supporting role. The war in Italy is over but some German troops are still not accounted for. Australian troops <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Tarakan_(1945)" title="Battle of Tarakan (1945)">land on Tarakan island</a> off the coast of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Borneo" title="Borneo">Borneo</a></dd>

May 2, 1945
-Soviet forces capture the Reichstag building and install the Soviet flag. The Battle of Berlin ends when German General Helmuth Weidling, commander of the Berlin Defence Area, (and no longer bound by Goebbels's commands), unconditionally surrenders the city of Berlin to Soviet General Vasily Chuikov. General Vietinghoff surrenders his troops in Northern Italy.
-<dd> Soviet forces capture the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Reichstag_building" title="Reichstag building">Reichstag building</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Raising_a_flag_over_the_Reichstag" title="Raising a flag over the Reichstag">install the Soviet flag</a>. The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Berlin" title="Battle of Berlin">Battle of Berlin</a> ends when German General <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Helmuth_Weidling" title="Helmuth Weidling">Helmuth Weidling</a>, commander of the Berlin Defence Area, (and no longer bound by Goebbels's commands), unconditionally surrenders the city of Berlin to Soviet General Vasily Chuikov. General Vietinghoff surrenders his troops in Northern Italy.</dd>

-Rangoon is liberated. The German cruiser Admiral Hipper is scuttled, having been hit heavily by the RAF in April. Éamon de Valera, Taoiseach (prime minister) of Ireland, offers regrets for Hitler's death to German officialdom.

May 5, 1942
-In the Coral Sea, both Japanese and American carrier aircraft spend this day and the following one searching for each other's ships, with no success, even though at one point the opposing carrier groups are separated by less than a hundred miles of ocean.

May 5, 1945
-Formal negotiations for Germany's surrender begin at Reims, France. Czech resistance fighters begin the Prague uprising and the Soviets begin the Prague Offensive. German troops in the Netherlands officially surrender; Prince Bernhard of the Netherlands accepts the surrender. Mauthausen concentration camp is liberated. Kamikazes have major successes off Okinawa. Japanese fire balloons claim their first and only lives—a Sunday school group in Bly, Oregon.
-<dd> Formal negotiations for Germany's surrender begin at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Reims" title="Reims">Reims</a>, France. <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_resistance" title="Czech resistance">Czech resistance</a> fighters begin the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Prague_uprising" title="Prague uprising">Prague uprising</a> and the Soviets begin the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Prague_Offensive" title="Prague Offensive">Prague Offensive</a>. German troops in the Netherlands officially surrender; Prince Bernhard of the Netherlands accepts the surrender. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mauthausen_concentration_camp" title="Mauthausen concentration camp">Mauthausen concentration camp</a> is liberated. Kamikazes have major successes off Okinawa. Japanese <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fire_balloon" title="Fire balloon">fire balloons</a> claim their first and only lives—a Sunday school group in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bly,_Oregon" title="Bly, Oregon">Bly, Oregon</a>.</dd>
May 6, 1941
-With much of the Iraqi air force destroyed and facing regular bombardment themselves, the Iraqi ground forces besieging RAF Habbaniya withdraw. The Luftwaffe arranges to send a small force to Iraq.

May 6, 1942
-General Stilwell abandons his trucks, which constantly become stuck and so are actually impeding progress rather than aiding it. He retains his Jeeps, which do better. Late in the day his party arrives at Indaw.

May 6, 1942
-On Corregidor, Lt. General Jonathan M. Wainwright surrenders the last U.S. forces in the Philippines to Lt. General Masaharu Homma. About 12,000 are made prisoners. Homma will soon face criticism from his superiors over the amount of time it has taken him to reduce the Philippines, and be forced into retirement (1943).
