June 13, 1942
-'Black Saturday' for the 8th Army at the Battle of Gazala; during the course of the day Rommel does great damage to the British armour. At the end of the day not only have unsustainably large amounts of British armour been destroyed, but both 50th Division and 1st South African Division, who have largely retained their forward positions along the Gazala Line, are threatened with envelopment. The position of 50th Division is especially grave since Rommel's armour now ranges freely between them and safety.
-<dd> 'Black Saturday' for the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eighth_Army_(United_Kingdom)" title="Eighth Army (United Kingdom)">8th Army</a> at the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Gazala" title="Battle of Gazala">Battle of Gazala</a>; during the course of the day Rommel does great damage to the British armour. At the end of the day not only have unsustainably large amounts of British armour been destroyed, but both <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/50th_(Northumbrian)_Infantry_Division" title="50th (Northumbrian) Infantry Division">50th Division</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/1st_Infantry_Division_(South_Africa)" title="1st Infantry Division (South Africa)">1st South African Division</a>, who have largely retained their forward positions along the Gazala Line, are threatened with envelopment. The position of 50th Division is especially grave since Rommel's armour now ranges freely between them and safety.</dd>

June 13, 1944
-Germany launches a V1 Flying Bomb attack on England, in Hitler's view a kind of revenge for the invasion. He believes in Germany's victory with this "secret weapon." The V-1 attacks will continue through October, when the last launch site is taken by Allied forces. The U.S. Naval bombardment of Saipan begins. In response, Admiral Toyoda Soemu, commander-in-chief of the Imperial Japanese Navy, orders his fleet to attack U.S. Navy forces around Saipan.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a> launches a <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/V1_Flying_Bomb" title="V1 Flying Bomb">V1 Flying Bomb</a> attack on <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/England" title="England">England</a>, in Hitler's view a kind of revenge for the invasion. He believes in Germany's victory with this "secret weapon." The V-1 attacks will continue through October, when the last launch site is taken by Allied forces. The U.S. Naval bombardment of Saipan begins. In response, Admiral Toyoda Soemu, commander-in-chief of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Imperial_Japanese_Navy" title="Imperial Japanese Navy">Imperial Japanese Navy</a>, orders his fleet to attack U.S. Navy forces around Saipan.</dd>

June 14, 1940
-Paris occupied by German troops; Elements of the French Navy (Marine Nationale) based in Toulon carried out offensive operations against Italian targets along the Ligurian coast. A total military blockade on the Baltic States by the Soviet Baltic Fleet. Soviet troops along the Baltic borders are ready to organise communist coups in the Baltic States. Soviet bombers shoot down a Finnish passenger airplane Kaleva flying from Tallinn to Helsinki and carrying three diplomatic pouches from the U.S. legations in Tallinn, Riga and Helsinki.
-<dd> Paris occupied by German troops; Elements of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_Navy" title="French Navy">French Navy</a> (<i>Marine Nationale</i>) based in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Toulon" title="Toulon">Toulon</a> carried out offensive operations against Italian targets along the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Liguria" title="Liguria">Ligurian coast</a>. A total military blockade on the Baltic States by the Soviet <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Baltic_Fleet" title="Baltic Fleet">Baltic Fleet</a>. Soviet troops along the Baltic borders are ready to organise communist coups in the Baltic States. Soviet bombers shoot down a Finnish passenger airplane <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kaleva_(airplane)" title="Kaleva (airplane)"><i>Kaleva</i></a> flying from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tallinn" title="Tallinn">Tallinn</a> to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Helsinki" title="Helsinki">Helsinki</a> and carrying three diplomatic pouches from the U.S. legations in Tallinn, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Riga" title="Riga">Riga</a> and Helsinki.</dd>
June 14, 1941
-All German and Italian assets in the United States are frozen. 10,100 people from Estonia, 15,000 from Latvia and 34,000 (or 35,000, starting a day earlier) from Lithuania are deported to Siberia by the Soviet Union.
-<dd> All German and Italian assets in the United States are frozen. 10,100 people from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Estonia" title="Estonia">Estonia</a>, 15,000 from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvia" title="Latvia">Latvia</a> and 34,000 (or 35,000, starting a day earlier) from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuania" title="Lithuania">Lithuania</a> are deported to Siberia by the Soviet Union.</dd>
June 14, 1942
-At the Gazala Line, the British position has become untenable, and General Auchinleck authorizes General Ritchie to make a concerted withdrawal from forward positions along the line.
-<dd> At <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Gazala" title="Battle of Gazala">the Gazala Line</a>, the British position has become untenable, and General <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Claude_Auchinleck" title="Claude Auchinleck">Auchinleck</a> authorizes General <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Neil_Ritchie" title="Neil Ritchie">Ritchie</a> to make a concerted withdrawal from forward positions along the line.</dd>
June 14, 1942
-1st South African Division is able to withdraw along the coastal road, but the road cannot accommodate all the troops at once, and this route is in any event is under threat of being cut by Rommel's forces; so troops including 50th Division must first breakout to the southwest, through the area occupied by Italian X Corps, and then turn east to rejoin 8th Army. This somewhat daring operation is concluded successfully. The RAF forces available, although outnumbered, make a valiant effort to cover the retreat. Churchill sends Auchinleck a telegram beginning, 'To what position does Ritchie want to withdraw the Gazala troops? Presume there is no question in any case of giving up Tobruk.'
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/1st_Infantry_Division_(South_Africa)" title="1st Infantry Division (South Africa)">1st South African Division</a> is able to withdraw along the coastal road, but the road cannot accommodate all the troops at once, and this route is in any event is under threat of being cut by Rommel's forces; so troops including <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/50th_(Northumbrian)_Infantry_Division" title="50th (Northumbrian) Infantry Division">50th Division</a> must first breakout to the southwest, through the area occupied by Italian X Corps, and then turn east to rejoin <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eighth_Army_(United_Kingdom)" title="Eighth Army (United Kingdom)">8th Army</a>. This somewhat daring operation is concluded successfully. The RAF forces available, although outnumbered, make a valiant effort to cover the retreat. <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Churchill" title="Churchill">Churchill</a> sends Auchinleck a telegram beginning, 'To what position does Ritchie want to withdraw the Gazala troops? Presume there is no question in any case of giving up Tobruk.'</dd>
June 14, 1942
-The convoy 'Vigorous', en route to Malta, sights a large Italian naval squadron headed toward it. 'Harpoon' comes under attack for the first time; 'Vigorous' has been under air attack almost since leaving port.
-<dd> The convoy <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Vigorous" title="Operation Vigorous">'Vigorous'</a>, en route to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Siege_of_Malta_(World_War_II)" title="Siege of Malta (World War II)">Malta</a>, sights a large Italian naval squadron headed toward it. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Harpoon_(1942)" title="Operation Harpoon (1942)">'Harpoon'</a> comes under attack for the first time; 'Vigorous' has been under air attack almost since leaving port.</dd>
June 15, 1940
-Eight-hour ultimatum to surrender is given to Lithuania by the Soviets. President Smetona escapes from the country so the takeover is not possible to do in a formally legal way. Soviet troops enter Lithuania and attack Latvian border guards. Start of the evacuation of British troops from ports in western France in Operation Ariel.
-<dd> Eight-hour ultimatum to surrender is given to Lithuania by the Soviets. President Smetona escapes from the country so the takeover is not possible to do in a formally legal way. Soviet troops enter Lithuania and attack Latvian border guards. Start of the evacuation of British troops from ports in western France in <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Ariel" title="Operation Ariel">Operation Ariel</a>.</dd>
June 15, 1941
-British Operation Battleaxe attempts and fails to relieve the Siege of Tobruk. The British are heavily defeated at Halfaya Pass nicknamed "Hell-fire pass".
-<dd> British <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Battleaxe" title="Operation Battleaxe">Operation Battleaxe</a> attempts and fails to relieve the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Siege_of_Tobruk" title="Siege of Tobruk">Siege of Tobruk</a>. The British are heavily defeated at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Halfaya_Pass" title="Halfaya Pass">Halfaya Pass</a> nicknamed "Hell-fire pass".</dd>
June 15, 1942
-General Auchinleck sends Churchill a reply to the latter's telegram of the 14th, saying in part, "...I have no intention whatever of giving up Tobruk."
-<dd> General <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Claude_Auchinleck" title="Claude Auchinleck">Auchinleck</a> sends <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Churchill" title="Churchill">Churchill</a> a reply to the latter's telegram of the 14th, saying in part, "...I have no intention whatever of giving up Tobruk."</dd>

-Osaka, Japan, is heavily bombed.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Osaka" title="Osaka">Osaka</a>, Japan, is heavily bombed.</dd>
June 16, 1940
-Philippe Pétain becomes premier of France upon the resignation of Reynaud's government. The French sloop La Curieuse forces the Italian submarine Provano to surface and then sinks it by ramming. Soviet Union gives eight-hour ultimatum to Latvia and Estonia to surrender.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Philippe_P%C3%A9tain" title="Philippe Pétain">Philippe Pétain</a> becomes premier of France upon the resignation of Reynaud's government. The French sloop <a class="new" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=French_sloop_La_Curieuse&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="French sloop La Curieuse (page does not exist)"><i>La Curieuse</i></a> forces the Italian submarine <i>Provano</i> to surface and then sinks it by ramming. Soviet Union gives eight-hour ultimatum to Latvia and Estonia to surrender.</dd>
June 16, 1941
-All German and Italian consulates in the United States are ordered closed and their staffs to leave the country by July 10.
-<dd> All German and Italian consulates in the United States are ordered closed and their staffs to leave the country by July 10.</dd>
June 16, 1942
-Two convoys moving toward Malta suffer heavy losses; German air forces continue to bomb the island itself. Operation Harpoon arrives in Malta, but only two of the six supply ships survive; one of them has lost part of its cargo due to mine damage. The sinking of the tanker Kentucky means that there will be precious little aviation fuel added to the dwindling RAF stocks on Malta. Late in the day, Operation Vigorous is cancelled; the convoy diverts back to Alexandria.
-<dd> Two convoys moving toward Malta suffer heavy losses; German air forces continue to bomb the island itself. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Harpoon_(1942)" title="Operation Harpoon (1942)">Operation Harpoon</a> arrives in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Siege_of_Malta_(World_War_II)" title="Siege of Malta (World War II)">Malta</a>, but only two of the six supply ships survive; one of them has lost part of its cargo due to mine damage. The sinking of the tanker <i>Kentucky</i> means that there will be precious little aviation fuel added to the dwindling RAF stocks on Malta. Late in the day, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Vigorous" title="Operation Vigorous">Operation Vigorous</a> is cancelled; the convoy diverts back to Alexandria.</dd>
June 16, 1942
-Churchill, about to leave for America, takes the unusual step of sending a letter to King George VI, advising him to make Anthony Eden Prime Minister should Churchill not survive the journey.
-<dd> <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Churchill" title="Churchill">Churchill</a>, about to leave for America, takes the unusual step of sending a letter to King George VI, advising him to make <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anthony_Eden" title="Anthony Eden">Anthony Eden</a> Prime Minister should Churchill not survive the journey.</dd>

June 18, 1940
-General De Gaulle forms the Comité français de la Libération nationale, a French government in exile; Estonia, Latvia and Lithuania are occupied by the Soviet Union.

June 19, 1944
-[19-20] The Battle of the Philippine Sea, nicknamed the Great Marianas Turkey Shoot by Americans, takes place. The United States Fifth Fleet wins a decisive naval battle over the Imperial Japanese Navy near the Mariana Islands. Over 200 Japanese planes are shot down while the Americans only lose 29 to enemy action.[2][3][16][17]
-<dd> The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_the_Philippine_Sea" title="Battle of the Philippine Sea">Battle of the Philippine Sea</a>, nicknamed the Great Marianas Turkey Shoot by Americans, takes place. The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States_Fifth_Fleet" title="United States Fifth Fleet">United States Fifth Fleet</a> wins a decisive naval battle over the Imperial Japanese Navy near the Mariana Islands. Over 200 Japanese planes are shot down while the Americans only lose 29 to enemy action.</dd>
June 19, 1944
-A severe Channel storm destroys one of the Allies' Mulberry harbours in Normandy. The Red Army prepares for "Operation Bagration," a huge offensive in Byelorussia (White Russia).
-<dd> A severe Channel storm destroys one of the Allies' <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mulberry_harbour" title="Mulberry harbour">Mulberry harbours</a> in Normandy. The Red Army prepares for "Operation Bagration," a huge offensive in Byelorussia (White Russia).</dd>

June 20, 1941
-Under the directives of the United States Department of War, the bulk of the personnel of what had been known as the United States Army Air Corps up to this date are brought into what becomes the United States Army Air Forces from this date forward, with General Henry H. Arnold as its first commander. As part of the reorganization, General Headquarters Air Force is renamed Air Force Combat Command; the new Army Air Forces organization consists of Air Force Combat Command (its combat element), with the existing logistics and training element retaining the older "United States Army Air Corps" designation.
-<dd> Under the directives of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States_Department_of_War" title="United States Department of War">United States Department of War</a>, the bulk of the personnel of what had been known as the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States_Army_Air_Corps" title="United States Army Air Corps">United States Army Air Corps</a> up to this date are brought into what becomes the <b><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States_Army_Air_Forces" title="United States Army Air Forces">United States Army Air Forces</a></b> from this date forward, with <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/General_officer" title="General officer">General</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_H._Arnold" title="Henry H. Arnold">Henry H. Arnold</a> as its first commander. As part of the reorganization, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States_Army_Air_Corps#GHQ_Air_Force" title="United States Army Air Corps">General Headquarters Air Force</a> is renamed Air Force Combat Command; the new Army Air Forces organization consists of Air Force Combat Command (its combat element), with the existing logistics and training element retaining the older "United States Army Air Corps" designation.</dd>
June 20, 1944
-[19-20] The Battle of the Philippine Sea, nicknamed the Great Marianas Turkey Shoot by Americans, takes place. Over 200 Japanese planes are shot down while the Americans only lose 29 to enemy action.[2][3][16][17]
-<dd> The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_the_Philippine_Sea" title="Battle of the Philippine Sea">Battle of the Philippine Sea</a>, nicknamed the Great Marianas Turkey Shoot by Americans, takes place. June 21, 1940
-The French battleship Lorraine opened fire on the Italian port of Bardia in Italian North Africa. During some of the last actions of the French against the Italians, French naval aircraft attacked Taranto and Livorno in mainland Italy.
-<dd> The French battleship <i>Lorraine</i> opened fire on the Italian port of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bardia" title="Bardia">Bardia</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_North_Africa" title="Italian North Africa">Italian North Africa</a>. June 21, 1940
-Soviet-led coups in the Baltic States. In the only military resistance in Tallinn, 2 die on Estonian side and about 10 on the Soviet side.

June 21, 1942
-Afrika Korps recaptures Tobruk, with 35,000 men captured; the road to Egypt is now open as the British retreat deep into Egypt. Tobruk's loss is a grievous blow to British morale. German land forces have been assisted by Luftwaffe attacks.
-<dd> Afrika Korps recaptures Tobruk, with 35,000 men captured; the road to Egypt is now open as the British retreat deep into Egypt. Tobruk's loss is a grievous blow to British morale. German land forces have been assisted by Luftwaffe attacks.</dd>
June 21, 1943
-Operation Cartwheel opens with landings by the United States 4th Marine Raider Battalion at Segi Point on New Georgia in the Solomon Islands, beginning the New Georgia Campaign. It will not be secured until August.

June 22, 1940

June 22, 1941
-Germany invades the Soviet Union with Operation Barbarossa, a three-pronged operation aimed at Leningrad, Moscow, and the southern oil fields of the Caucasus, ending the Molotov–Ribbentrop Pact. Romania invades south-western border areas of the Soviet Union in Europe on the side of Germany. British general in Libya/Egypt Wavell is replaced by General Auchinleck. June Uprising against the Soviet Union in Lithuania.
-<dd> Germany invades the Soviet Union with <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Barbarossa" title="Operation Barbarossa">Operation Barbarossa</a>, a three-pronged operation aimed at Leningrad, Moscow, and the southern oil fields of the Caucasus, ending the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Molotov%E2%80%93Ribbentrop_Pact" title="Molotov–Ribbentrop Pact">Molotov–Ribbentrop Pact</a>. Romania invades south-western border areas of the Soviet Union in Europe on the side of Germany. British general in Libya/Egypt Wavell is replaced by General Auchinleck. <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_1941_independence" title="Lithuanian 1941 independence">June Uprising</a> against the Soviet Union in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuania" title="Lithuania">Lithuania</a>.</dd>
June 22, 1944
-V-1s continue to hit England, especially London, sometimes with horrifying losses. Operation Bagration General attack by Soviet forces to clear the German forces from Belarus This results in the destruction of the German Army Group Centre, possibly the greatest defeat of the Wehrmacht during World War II. In the Burma Campaign, the Battle of Kohima ends with a British victory.
-<dd> V-1s continue to hit England, especially London, sometimes with horrifying losses. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Bagration" title="Operation Bagration">Operation Bagration</a>: General attack by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet</a> forces to clear the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">German</a> forces from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarus" title="Belarus">Belarus</a> This results in the destruction of the German <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Army_Group_Centre" title="Army Group Centre">Army Group Centre</a>, possibly the greatest defeat of the Wehrmacht during World War II. In the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Burma_Campaign" title="Burma Campaign">Burma Campaign</a>, the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Kohima" title="Battle of Kohima">Battle of Kohima</a> ends with a British victory.</dd>
June 23, 1941
-In the late evening, Hitler first arrives at his headquarters at Rastenburg, East Prussia, codenamed "Wolf's Lair" (Wolfsschanze). Between this date and November 20, 1944, Hitler will have spent 800 days at Wolf's Lair. German troops massacre 42 at Ablinga.
-<dd> In the late evening, Hitler first arrives at his headquarters at <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rastenburg" title="Rastenburg">Rastenburg</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/East_Prussia" title="East Prussia">East Prussia</a>, codenamed "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wolf%27s_Lair" title="Wolf's Lair">Wolf's Lair</a>" (Wolfsschanze). Between this date and November 20, 1944, Hitler will have spent 800 days at Wolf's Lair. German troops massacre 42 at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ablinga" title="Ablinga">Ablinga</a>.</dd>
June 23, 1943
-American troops land in the Trobriand Islands, close to New Guinea. The American strategy of driving up the Southwest Pacific by "Island Hopping" continues.

The American strategy of driving up the Southwest Pacific by "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Island_hopping" title="Island hopping">Island Hopping</a>" continues.</dd>

-France officially surrenders to Germany at 0135. Last major evacuation of Operation Ariel; 191,870 Allied soldiers, airmen and some civilians had escaped from France.

July 2, 1941
-Ponary massacre killings begin, with the shooting of Soviet POWs captured during Operation Barbarossa, which began two weeks earlier, and with the deportation of hundreds of Jews from Vilnius to Soviet dug fuel tank pits near the Ponariai suburb of Vilnius, where they are shot or buried alive. Reports by survivors are accepted as hallucinations. The mass deportations and shooting of Jews continued until 1943. Hungarian troops take over Stanisławów and other towns in what is now Ukraine.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ponary_massacre" title="Ponary massacre">Ponary massacre</a> killings begin, with the shooting of Soviet POWs captured during <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Barbarossa" title="Operation Barbarossa">Operation Barbarossa</a>, which began two weeks earlier, and with the deportation of hundreds of Jews from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vilnius" title="Vilnius">Vilnius</a> to Soviet dug fuel tank pits near the Ponariai suburb of Vilnius, where they are shot or buried alive. Reports by survivors are accepted as hallucinations. The mass deportations and shooting of Jews continued until 1943. Hungarian troops take over Stanisławów and other towns in what is now Ukraine.</dd>

July 3, 1941
-Stalin announces a "scorched earth policy". The United States of America elevates its General Headquarters, United States Army in order to command and plan for military operations within the Zone of the Interior. Italian General Pietro Gazzera surrenders the remnants of his forces in the Jimma area. British troops employ brave and risky flanking tactics to win the Battle of Deir ez-Zor.
-<dd> Stalin announces a "scorched earth policy". Italian General <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pietro_Gazzera" title="Pietro Gazzera">Pietro Gazzera</a> surrenders the remnants of his forces in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jimma" title="Jimma">Jimma area</a>. July 3, 1944
-Minsk in Belarus is liberated by Soviet forces.  The Allies find themselves in the "battle of the hedgerows", as they are stymied by the agricultural hedges in Western France which intelligence had not properly evaluated. Various impromptu devices and inventions, often made out of cut-up German "hedgehog" shore defense devices and mounted to Allied tanks, are designed and made to successfully deal with the matter. Siena, Italy falls to Algerian troops of the French forces.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Minsk" title="Minsk">Minsk</a> in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarus" title="Belarus">Belarus</a> is liberated by Soviet forces. The Allies find themselves in the "battle of the hedgerows", as they are stymied by the agricultural hedges in Western France which intelligence had not properly evaluated. Various impromptu devices and inventions, often made out of cut-up German "hedgehog" shore defense devices and mounted to Allied tanks, are designed and made to successfully deal with the matter. Siena, Italy falls to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Algeria" title="Algeria">Algerian</a> troops of the French forces.</dd>
July 4, 1940
-The destruction of the French Fleet at Mers-el-Kébir, Algeria by the Royal Navy; Vichy French government breaks off diplomatic relations with Britain in protest.  At Alexandria the French agree to demilitarise the French battleship Lorraine and several smaller ships. The Duke of Windsor (tainted by suspicion of pro-Nazism) is named governor of the Bahamas, putting him some distance from controversy.
-<dd> The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Attack_on_Mers-el-K%C3%A9bir" title="Attack on Mers-el-Kébir">destruction of the French Fleet at Mers-el-Kébir</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Algeria" title="Algeria">Algeria</a> by the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">Royal Navy</a>; <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vichy_French" title="Vichy French">Vichy French</a> government breaks off diplomatic relations with Britain in protest. July 5, 1941

-Vitebsk (Belarus) is captured; this opens the battle of Smolensk, an important communications centre, considered by the German high command to be "the gateway to Moscow."

July 9, 1944

July 10, 1941
-The occupation of Latvia starts officially. Guderian's Panzers take Minsk; the Germans advance farther into Ukraine. Units of the Italian Expeditionary Corps in Russia begin to arrive. A legion from the Independent State of Croatia is part of the Italian corps.

At the start of the Soviet Narva Offensive, July 24–30, the Soviet 8th Army is beaten by the Estonian 45th Regiment and East Prussian 44th Regiment. The army detachment "Narwa" begins to retreat to the Tannenberg line. Majdanek Concentration Camp is liberated by Soviet forces, the first among many. The Soviet Union is now in control of several large cities in Poland, including Lublin. US bombers mistakenly bomb American troops near St. Lo, France.

July 27, 1944
-Battles on the Tannenberg Line. At the start of the battles there are 25 Estonian and 24 Dutch, Danish and Flemish infantry battalions on the German side at the Narva Front. The artillery forces, and the tank, engineer and other special units are composed mainly of Germans. The attack by the Soviet Armed Forces is stopped, tens of thousands of men are killed in both sides. The batteling would continue untill the 10th of August

July 28, 1941
-Japanese troops occupy southern French Indochina. The Vichy French colonial government is allowed by the Japanese to continue to administer Vietnam. French repression continues. The Vichy French also agree to the occupation by the Japanese of bases in Indochina. The Germans push against Smolensk, and in the meantime solidify their presence in the Baltic states; native Jewish populations of the Baltic states are being exterminated.

July 28, 1944
-The Red Army take Brest-Litovsk, the site of the Russo-German peace treaty in World War I. The first operational use of the Me 163B Komet rocket fighter occurs by units of JG 400 in defense of the Leuna synthetic fuel facilities, the Third Reich's largest synthetic fuels complex.
-<dd> The Red Army take <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brest-Litovsk" title="Brest-Litovsk">Brest-Litovsk</a>, the site of the Russo-German peace treaty in World War I. August 1, 1940
-[1-31] The so-called Spéngelskrich ("War of Pin-badges") begins in occupied Luxembourg as civilians wear patriotic lapel badges prominently, in defiance of Nazi attempts to "Germanize" the territory.

August 1, 1940
-Hitler sets 15 September as the date for Operation Sea Lion, the invasion of Britain.  Soviet Foreign Minister Molotov reaffirms Molotov-Ribbentrop pact in the Soviet Supreme while verbally attacking both Britain and the USA. He also asserts that the boundaries of the Soviet Union are moved to the shores of the Baltic Sea.  The Italian Royal Navy establishes its BETASOM submarine base in Bordeaux and joins the "Battle of the Atlantic."
-<dd> Hitler sets 15 September as the date for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Sea_Lion" title="Operation Sea Lion">Operation Sea Lion</a>, the invasion of Britain. Soviet Foreign Minister Molotov reaffirms Molotov-Ribbentrop pact in the Soviet Supreme while verbally attacking both Britain and the USA. He also asserts that the boundaries of the Soviet Union are moved to the shores of the Baltic Sea. The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Regia_Marina" title="Regia Marina">Italian Royal Navy</a> establishes its <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/BETASOM" title="BETASOM">BETASOM</a> submarine base in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bordeaux" title="Bordeaux">Bordeaux</a> and joins the "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_the_Atlantic" title="Battle of the Atlantic">Battle of the Atlantic</a>."</dd>

August 2, 1941
-All civilian radios in Norway confiscated by the German occupation. SS Commander Hans Krueger (alternative spelling, Hans Krüger) orders the registration of hundreds of Jewish and Polish intelligentsia in Stanisławów, who are subsequently tortured and murdered. This is the first implementation of the "one bullet one Jew" method in Galicia.
-<dd> All civilian radios in Norway confiscated by the German occupation. This is the first implementation of the "one bullet one Jew" method in Galicia.</dd>

-The Soviet Union declares war on Japan; the Soviet invasion of Manchuria begins about an hour later which includes landings on the Kuril Islands. The Japanese have been evacuating in anticipation of this.

-Franklin D. Roosevelt and Winston Churchill meet at NS Argentia, Newfoundland. The Atlantic Charter is created, signed, and released to the world press.

Roosevelt</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Winston_Churchill" title="Winston Churchill">Winston Churchill</a> meet at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Naval_Station_Argentia" title="Naval Station Argentia">NS Argentia</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dominion_of_Newfoundland" title="Dominion of Newfoundland">Newfoundland</a>. The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Atlantic_Charter" title="Atlantic Charter">Atlantic Charter</a> is created, signed, and released to the world press.</dd>

August 13, 1940
-This is "Adler Tag" or "Eagle Day".  Hermann Göring starts a two-week assault on British airfields in preparation for invasion. (For some German historians, this is the beginning of the "Battle of Britain.")

August 13, 1942
-General Bernard Montgomery appointed commander of the Eighth Army, which encompassed Allied ground forces in Egypt and Libya; Churchill is anxious to see more offensive action on the part of the Allies in North Africa.

August 14, 1940
-British scientist Sir Henry Tizard leaves for the United States on the Tizard Mission, giving over to the Americans a number of top secret British technologies including the magnetron, the secret device at the heart of radar. Radar is already proving itself in the defence of Britain.
-<dd> British scientist Sir <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_Tizard" title="Henry Tizard">Henry Tizard</a> leaves for the United States on the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tizard_Mission" title="Tizard Mission">Tizard Mission</a>, giving over to the Americans a number of top secret British technologies including the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Magnetron" title="Magnetron">magnetron</a>, the secret device at the heart of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Radar" title="Radar">radar</a>. August 14, 1944
-The failure of the Allies to close the Falaise pocket in France proves advantageous to the Germans fleeing to the east who escape the pincer movement of the Allies. A clash between Italian POWs and American servicemen ends in the Fort Lawton Riot

August 15, 1940

August 15, 1945
-Emperor Hirohito issues a radio broadcast announcing the Surrender of Japan; though the surrender seems to be "unconditional", the Emperor's status is still open for discussion. Victory over Japan Day celebrations take place worldwide.

-The Battle of Britain continues; Germans are hampered by poor aircraft range and British extensive use of RADAR.  A first draft of the Destroyers for Bases Agreement by the US and Britain is made public.

August 19, 1940
-Italian forces take Berbera, the capital of British Somaliland and the British defenders flee to Aden.  The fall of Berbera completes the invasion of the British colony.  By the end of the month, the Italians control British Somaliland and several towns and forts along the border with Sudan and Kenya including Kassala, Gallabat, and Moyale.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kingdom_of_Italy" title="Kingdom of Italy">Italian</a> forces take <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Berbera" title="Berbera">Berbera</a>, the capital of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_Somaliland" title="British Somaliland">British Somaliland</a> and the British defenders flee to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aden" title="Aden">Aden</a>.  The fall of Berbera completes the invasion of the British colony.  By the end of the month, the Italians control British Somaliland and several towns and forts along the border with <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Egyptian_Sudan" title="Anglo-Egyptian Sudan">Sudan</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kenya_Colony" title="Kenya Colony">Kenya</a> including <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kassala" title="Kassala">Kassala</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gallabat" title="Gallabat">Gallabat</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moyale" title="Moyale">Moyale</a>.</dd>

August 19, 1944
-The French Resistance begins an uprising in Paris, partly inspired by the Allied approach to the Seine River.  In a radio broadcast, Jüri Uluots, the acting Head of State of Estonia, calls the Estonian conscripts to hold the Soviet Armed Forces back until a peace treaty with Germany is signed.

August 19, 1945
-At a spontaneous non-communist meeting in Hanoi, Ho Chi Minh and the Viet Minh assume a leading role in the movement to wrest power from the French. With the Japanese still in control of Indochina in the interim, Bảo Đại goes along because he thought that the Viet Minh were still working with the American OSS and could guarantee independence for Vietnam. Later, Ho Chi Minh's guerrillas occupy Hanoi and proclaim a provisional government. Hostilities between Chinese Nationalists and Chinese Communists break into the open.
-<dd> At a spontaneous non-communist meeting in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hanoi" title="Hanoi">Hanoi</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ho_Chi_Minh" title="Ho Chi Minh">Ho Chi Minh</a> and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Viet_Minh" title="Viet Minh">Viet Minh</a> assume a leading role in the movement to wrest power from the French. Later, Ho Chi Minh's guerrillas occupy Hanoi and proclaim a provisional government. Hostilities between Chinese Nationalists and Chinese Communists break into the open.</dd>

August 22, 1942
-Brazil declares war on the Axis countries, partly in response to numerous riots by a populace angry at the sinking of Brazilian ships.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a> declares war on the Axis countries, partly in response to numerous riots by a populace angry at the sinking of Brazilian ships.</dd>
August 22, 1942
-Massacre of Jews at Stanislau, Poland (later Ivano-Frankivsk, Ukraine) in what the Nazi authorities describe as a "reprisal action", 1,000 Jews are shot, including women and girls who are raped beforehand at Gestapo headquarters; the head of the Judenrat(Mordechai Goldstein) is hanged publicly, along with 20 members of the Jewish police.
-<dd> Massacre of Jews at <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stanislavov" title="Stanislavov">Stanislau</a>, Poland (later Ivano-Frankivsk, Ukraine): in what the Nazi authorities describe as a "reprisal action", 1,000 Jews are shot, including women and girls who are raped beforehand at <i>Gestapo</i> headquarters; the head of the <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Judenrat" title="Judenrat">Judenrat</a></i>(Mordechai Goldstein) is hanged publicly, along with 20 members of the Jewish police.</dd>
August 22, 1944
-The Japanese are now in total retreat from India. German Chancellor Adolf Hitler issued the first of several orders to the German commander of Paris, General Dietrich von Choltitz, to destroy the city.
-<dd> The Japanese are now in total retreat from India. German Chancellor Adolf Hitler issued the first of several orders to the German commander of Paris, General Dietrich von Choltitz, to destroy the city.</dd>

August 23, 1943
-Operation Polkovodets Rumyantsev liberates Kharkov, Ukraine. The Battle of Kursk has become the first successful major Soviet summer offensive of the war.
-<dd> <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Polkovodets_Rumyantsev" title="Operation Polkovodets Rumyantsev">Operation Polkovodets Rumyantsev</a> liberates <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kharkiv" title="Kharkiv">Kharkov</a>, Ukraine. The Battle of Kursk has become the first successful major Soviet summer offensive of the war.</dd>

-Romania breaks with the Axis, surrenders to the Soviet Union, and joins the Allies.

August 25, 1940
-Churchill orders the bombing of Berlin in retaliation for the previous night's bombing of Cripplegate.

August 25, 1941
-British and Soviet troops invade Iran to save the Abadan oilfields and the important railways and routes to Soviet Union for the supply of war material.

August 25, 1944
-Paris is liberated; De Gaulle makes a triumphant speech at the Hotel de la Ville, which is also broadcast nationwide.  The German military under Lt. Gen. von Choltitz disobeys Hitler's orders to burn the city and destroy all bridges over the Seine. Meanwhile the southern Allied forces move up from the Riviera, take Grenoble and Avignon.
-<dd> Paris is liberated; De Gaulle makes a triumphant speech at the Hotel de la Ville, which is also broadcast nationwide.  The German military under Lt. Gen. von Choltitz disobeys Hitler's orders to burn the city and destroy all bridges over the Seine. Meanwhile the southern Allied forces move up from the Riviera, take <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Grenoble" title="Grenoble">Grenoble</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Avignon" title="Avignon">Avignon</a>.</dd>

August 30, 1940
-The bombing of England continues; London is now bombed in retaliation for the bombing of Berlin; thus, the beginning of "the London Blitz."  Adolf Hitler and Benito Mussolini dictated the so-called Second Vienna Award which forced Romania to hand over the Northern Transylvania (including the entire Maramureș and part of Crișana) to Hungary.
-<dd> The bombing of England continues; London is now bombed in retaliation for the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bombing_of_Berlin" title="Bombing of Berlin">bombing of Berlin</a>; thus, the beginning of "the London Blitz." : Adolf Hitler and Benito Mussolini dictated the so-called <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Second_Vienna_Award" title="Second Vienna Award">Second Vienna Award</a> which forced Romania to hand over the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Northern_Transylvania" title="Northern Transylvania">Northern Transylvania</a> (including the entire <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maramure%C8%99" title="Maramureș">Maramureș</a> and part of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cri%C8%99ana" title="Crișana">Crișana</a>) to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hungary" title="Hungary">Hungary</a>.</dd>
August 30, 1941
-The Shetland bus, a clandestine special operations group that made a permanent link between Shetland, Scotland and German-occupied Norway, begins operations.
-<dd> The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shetland_bus" title="Shetland bus">Shetland bus</a>, a clandestine special operations group that made a permanent link between Shetland, Scotland and German-occupied Norway, begins operations.</dd>
August 30, 1942
-The Battle of Alam Halfa, a few miles south of El Alamein begins. This will be Rommel's last attempt to break through the Allied lines in Egypt; the air superiority of the Desert Air Force will play a significant role for the Allies.
-<dd> The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Alam_el_Halfa" title="Battle of Alam el Halfa">Battle of Alam Halfa</a>, a few miles south of El Alamein begins. This will be Rommel's last attempt to break through the Allied lines in Egypt; the air superiority of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Desert_Air_Force" title="Desert Air Force">Desert Air Force</a> will play a significant role for the Allies.</dd>

September 1, 1939
-The Republic of China and the Empire of Japan are involved in the early stages of the third year of armed conflict between them during the Second Sino-Japanese War. The war is in what will be known as the "Second Period", which starts in October 1938 and ends in December 1941. This conflict will eventually be swept up into World War II when Japan joins the Axis and China joins the Allies.
-<dd> The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Republic_of_China_(1912%E2%80%931949)" title="Republic of China (1912–1949)">Republic of China</a> and the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Empire_of_Japan" title="Empire of Japan">Empire of Japan</a> are involved in the early stages of the third year of armed conflict between them during the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Second_Sino-Japanese_War" title="Second Sino-Japanese War">Second Sino-Japanese War</a>. The war is in what will be known as the "Second Period", which starts in October 1938 and ends in December 1941. This conflict will eventually be swept up into <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a> when Japan joins the Axis and China joins the Allies.</dd>
September 1, 1939
-The Invasion of Poland by Nazi Germany starts at 445 a.m. with the Luftwaffe attacking several targets in Poland. The Luftwaffe launches air attacks against Kraków, Łódź, and Warsaw. Within five minutes of the Luftwaffe attacks, Nazi Germany's Kriegsmarine orders the old Battleship Schleswig-Holstein to open fire on the Polish military transit depot at Westerplatte in the Free City of Danzig on the Baltic Sea, but the attack is repulsed. By 800 a.m., troops of the German Army, still without a formal declaration of war issued, launch an attack near the Polish town of Mokra.
-<dd> The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Invasion_of_Poland" title="Invasion of Poland">Invasion of Poland</a> by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nazi_Germany" title="Nazi Germany">Nazi Germany</a> starts at 4:45 a.m. with the <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luftwaffe" title="Luftwaffe">Luftwaffe</a></i> attacking several targets in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Second_Polish_Republic" title="Second Polish Republic">Poland</a>. The <i>Luftwaffe</i> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bombing_of_Warsaw_in_World_War_II" title="Bombing of Warsaw in World War II">launches air attacks</a> against <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Krak%C3%B3w" title="Kraków">Kraków</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/%C5%81%C3%B3d%C5%BA" title="Łódź">Łódź</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Warsaw" title="Warsaw">Warsaw</a>. Within five minutes of the <i>Luftwaffe</i> attacks, Nazi Germany's <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kriegsmarine" title="Kriegsmarine">Kriegsmarine</a></i> orders the old <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battleship" title="Battleship">Battleship</a> <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SMS_Schleswig-Holstein" title="SMS Schleswig-Holstein">Schleswig-Holstein</a></i> to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Westerplatte" title="Battle of Westerplatte">open fire</a> on the Polish military transit depot at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Westerplatte" title="Battle of Westerplatte">Westerplatte</a> in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Free_City_of_Danzig" title="Free City of Danzig">Free City of Danzig</a> on the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Baltic_Sea" title="Baltic Sea">Baltic Sea</a>, but the attack is repulsed. By 8:00 a.m., troops of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_Army_(Wehrmacht)" title="German Army (Wehrmacht)">German Army</a>, still without a formal declaration of war issued, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Mokra" title="Battle of Mokra">launch an attack near the Polish town of Mokra</a>.</dd>
September 1, 1939
-Norway and Switzerland declare their neutrality.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norway" title="Norway">Norway</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Switzerland</a> declare their <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Neutral_country" title="Neutral country">neutrality</a>.</dd>
September 1, 1939
-The British government declares general mobilization of the British Armed Forces and starts evacuation plans in preparation of German air attacks.

September 1, 1941
-With the assistance of Finnish armies in the north, Leningrad is now completely cut off. A pro-German Government of National Salvation formed in the Territory of the Military Commander in Serbia under Milan Nedić. All Jews under German rule must wear the yellow star of David badge with "Jew" clearly written in it, are forbidden to live with or marry non-Jews, and are forbidden to leave their towns without written consent, in accordance with the Nuremberg Laws of 1935. The decree, signed by Heydrich, is to take effect on September 19.
-<dd> With the assistance of Finnish armies in the north, Leningrad is now completely cut off. A pro-German <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Government_of_National_Salvation" title="Government of National Salvation">Government of National Salvation</a> formed in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Territory_of_the_Military_Commander_in_Serbia" title="Territory of the Military Commander in Serbia">Territory of the Military Commander in Serbia</a> under <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Milan_Nedi%C4%87" title="Milan Nedić">Milan Nedić</a>. All Jews under German rule must wear the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yellow_badge" title="Yellow badge">yellow star of David badge</a> with "Jew" clearly written in it, are forbidden to live with or marry non-Jews, and are forbidden to leave their towns without written consent, in accordance with the Nuremberg Laws of 1935. The decree, signed by Heydrich, is to take effect on September 19.</dd>

September 2, 1939
-The United Kingdom and France issue a joint ultimatum to Germany, requiring German troops to evacuate Polish territory; President Douglas Hyde of the Republic of Ireland declares the neutrality of his nation; the Swiss government orders a general mobilization of its forces.
-<dd> The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/France" title="France">France</a> issue a joint ultimatum to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a>, requiring German troops to evacuate <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Polish territory</a>; President <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Douglas_Hyde" title="Douglas Hyde">Douglas Hyde</a> of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Republic of Ireland</a> declares the neutrality of his nation; the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Swiss government</a> orders a general mobilization of its forces.</dd>
September 2, 1939
-The National Service (Armed Forces) Act 1939 is enacted immediately and enforces full conscription on all males between 18 and 41 resident in the UK.
-<dd> The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/National_Service_(Armed_Forces)_Act_1939" title="National Service (Armed Forces) Act 1939">National Service (Armed Forces) Act 1939</a> is enacted immediately and enforces full conscription on all males between 18 and 41 resident in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">UK</a>.</dd>

-The Free City of Danzig is annexed by Germany. Resistors entrenched in the city's Polish Post Office are overwhelmed.

September 2, 1940
-The Destroyers for Bases Agreement is completed. Britain obtains 50 destroyers in exchange for giving the United States land grants in various British possessions for the establishment of US naval and air bases, on ninety-nine-year rent-free leases on bases in the Bahamas, Antigua, St. Lucia, Trinidad, Jamaica, and British Guiana.
-<dd> The <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Destroyers_for_Bases_Agreement" title="Destroyers for Bases Agreement">Destroyers for Bases Agreement</a> is completed. Britain obtains 50 destroyers in exchange for giving the United States land grants in various British possessions for the establishment of US naval and air bases, on ninety-nine-year rent-free leases on bases in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bahamas" title="Bahamas">Bahamas</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Antigua" title="Antigua">Antigua</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/St._Lucia" title="St. Lucia">St. Lucia</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Trinidad" title="Trinidad">Trinidad</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jamaica" title="Jamaica">Jamaica</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_Guiana" title="British Guiana">British Guiana</a>.</dd>
September 2, 1944
-Allied troops enter Belgium.

September 2, 1945
-The Japanese Instrument of Surrender is signed on the deck of the USS Missouri in Tokyo Bay. The commander of the Imperial Japanese Army General Tomoyuki Yamashita surrenders to Filipino and American troops at Kiangan, Ifugao in Northern Philippines. Ho Chi Minh issues his Proclamation of Independence, drawing heavily upon the American Declaration of Independence from a copy provided by the Office of Strategic Services. Ho declares himself president of the Democratic Republic of Vietnam and pursues American recognition but is repeatedly ignored by President Truman.
-<dd> The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_Instrument_of_Surrender" title="Japanese Instrument of Surrender">Japanese Instrument of Surrender</a> is signed on the deck of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/USS_Missouri_(BB-63)" title="USS Missouri (BB-63)">USS <i>Missouri</i></a> in Tokyo Bay. The commander of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Imperial_Japanese_Army" title="Imperial Japanese Army">Imperial Japanese Army</a> General <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tomoyuki_Yamashita" title="Tomoyuki Yamashita">Tomoyuki Yamashita</a> surrenders to Filipino and American troops at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kiangan,_Ifugao" title="Kiangan, Ifugao">Kiangan, Ifugao</a> in Northern <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>. Ho Chi Minh issues his <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proclamation_of_Independence_of_the_Democratic_Republic_of_Vietnam" title="Proclamation of Independence of the Democratic Republic of Vietnam">Proclamation of Independence</a>, drawing heavily upon the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_Declaration_of_Independence" title="American Declaration of Independence">American Declaration of Independence</a> from a copy provided by the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Office_of_Strategic_Services" title="Office of Strategic Services">Office of Strategic Services</a>. Ho declares himself president of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_Vietnam" title="Democratic Republic of Vietnam">Democratic Republic of Vietnam</a> and pursues American recognition but is repeatedly ignored by President Truman.</dd>
September 3, 1939
-At 1115 a.m. British Standard Time (BST), British Prime Minister Neville Chamberlain announces on BBC Radio that the deadline of the final British ultimatum for the withdrawal of German troops from Poland expired at 1100am and that "consequently this nation is at war with Germany". The Parliaments of Australia and New Zealand and the Viceroy of India also declare war on Germany within hours of Britain's declaration.
-<dd> At 11:15 a.m. <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_Standard_Time" title="British Standard Time">British Standard Time</a> (BST), British <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Prime_Minister" title="Prime Minister">Prime Minister</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Neville_Chamberlain" title="Neville Chamberlain">Neville Chamberlain</a> announces on <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/BBC_Radio" title="BBC Radio">BBC Radio</a> that the deadline of the final British ultimatum for the withdrawal of German troops from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Poland</a> expired at 11:00am and that "consequently this nation is at war with Germany". The Parliaments of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Zealand" title="New Zealand">New Zealand</a> and the Viceroy of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/India" title="India">India</a> also declare war on Germany within hours of Britain's declaration.</dd>
September 3, 1939
-At 1230pm BST the French Government delivers a similar final ultimatum; which expires at 300pm BST.
-<dd> At 12:30pm BST the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_Third_Republic" title="French Third Republic">French Government</a> delivers a similar final ultimatum; which expires at 3:00pm BST.</dd>
September 3, 1939
-Within hours of the British declaration of War, SS Athenia, a British cruise ship en route from Glasgow, Scotland to Montreal, Quebec, Canada is torpedoed by the German submarine U-30 250 miles (400 km) Northwest of Ireland. 112 passengers and crew members are killed. The "Battle of the Atlantic" starts.
-<dd> Within hours of the British declaration of War, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SS_Athenia_(1922)" title="SS Athenia (1922)">SS <i>Athenia</i></a>, a British cruise ship en route from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Glasgow" title="Glasgow">Glasgow, Scotland</a> to <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Montreal,_Quebec" title="Montreal, Quebec">Montreal, Quebec</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a> is torpedoed by the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/U-boat" title="U-boat">German submarine</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_submarine_U-30_(1936)" title="German submarine U-30 (1936)"><i>U-30</i></a> 250 miles (400 km) Northwest of Ireland. 112 passengers and crew members are killed. The "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_the_Atlantic" title="Battle of the Atlantic">Battle of the Atlantic</a>" starts.</dd>
September 3, 1939
-Bromberg massacre many ethnic German civilians are killed in the Polish city of Bromberg.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bloody_Sunday_(1939)" title="Bloody Sunday (1939)">Bromberg massacre</a>: many <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_minority_in_Poland" title="German minority in Poland">ethnic German civilians</a> are killed in the Polish city of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bydgoszcz" title="Bydgoszcz">Bromberg</a>.</dd>
September 3, 1940
-Hitler postpones the invasion of Britain, as the Luftwaffe fails to break the British defenses.  However, fears of the forthcoming invasion continue to haunt Britain.
-<dd> Hitler postpones the invasion of Britain, as the Luftwaffe fails to break the British defenses.  However, fears of the forthcoming invasion continue to haunt Britain.</dd>
September 3, 1941
-Murder of all 3,700 residents of the old Jewish quarter in Vilnius begins at the Ponary death site along with 10 members of the Judenrat. First written testimony of occurrences at Ponary by a survivor. Vilna Ghetto Jews required to hand over any gold or silver.
-<dd> Murder of all 3,700 residents of the old Jewish quarter in Vilnius begins at the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ponary_massacre" title="Ponary massacre">Ponary death site</a> along with 10 members of the Judenrat. First written testimony of occurrences at Ponary by a survivor. Vilna Ghetto Jews required to hand over any gold or silver.</dd>
September 3, 1942
-The Battle of Stalingrad proper may be said to have begun on this date, with German troops in the suburbs; even civilian men and boys are conscripted by the Red Army to assist in the defence.
-<dd> The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Stalingrad" title="Battle of Stalingrad">Battle of Stalingrad</a> proper may be said to have begun on this date, with German troops in the suburbs; even civilian men and boys are conscripted by the Red Army to assist in the defence.</dd>
September 3, 1943
-A secret Italian Armistice is signed and Italy drops out of the war. Mainland Italy is invaded when the British XXIII Corps lands at Reggio Calabria. Nazi Germany begins the evacuation of civilians from Berlin.
-<dd> A secret Italian Armistice is signed and Italy drops out of the war. Mainland <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a> is <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Allied_invasion_of_Italy" title="Allied invasion of Italy">invaded</a> when the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/XIII_Corps_(United_Kingdom)" title="XIII Corps (United Kingdom)">British XXIII Corps</a> lands at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Reggio_Calabria" title="Reggio Calabria">Reggio Calabria</a>. Nazi Germany begins the evacuation of civilians from Berlin.</dd>
September 3, 1944
-Brussels is liberated by the British Second Army. Lyon is liberated by French and American troops.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brussels" title="Brussels">Brussels</a> is liberated by the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_Second_Army" title="British Second Army">British Second Army</a>. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lyon" title="Lyon">Lyon</a> is liberated by French and American troops.</dd>
September 4, 1939
-At 800 a.m. Newfoundland Standard Time (NST), Dominion of Newfoundland declares war on Germany.
-<dd> At 8:00 a.m. <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Newfoundland_Standard_Time" title="Newfoundland Standard Time">Newfoundland Standard Time</a> (NST), <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dominion_of_Newfoundland" title="Dominion of Newfoundland">Dominion of Newfoundland</a> declares war on Germany.</dd>
September 4, 1939
-In the first British offensive action of the war, the Royal Air Force launch a raid on the German fleet in the Heligoland Bight. They target the German pocket-battleship Admiral Scheer anchored off Wilhelmshaven at the western end of the Kiel Canal. Several aircraft are lost in the attack and, although the German vessel is hit three times, all of the bombs fail to explode.
-<dd> In the first British offensive action of the war, the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Royal_Air_Force" title="Royal Air Force">Royal Air Force</a> launch a raid on the German fleet in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Heligoland_Bight" title="Heligoland Bight">Heligoland Bight</a>. They target the German pocket-battleship <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_pocket_battleship_Admiral_Scheer" title="German pocket battleship Admiral Scheer"><i>Admiral Scheer</i></a> anchored off <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wilhelmshaven" title="Wilhelmshaven">Wilhelmshaven</a> at the western end of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kiel_Canal" title="Kiel Canal">Kiel Canal</a>. Several aircraft are lost in the attack and, although the German vessel is hit three times, all of the bombs fail to explode.</dd>
September 4, 1939
-Japan announces its neutrality in the European situation. The British Admiralty announces the beginning of a naval blockade on Germany, one of a range of measures by which the British will wage economic warfare on the Axis powers.
-<dd> Japan announces its neutrality in the European situation. The British Admiralty announces the beginning of a naval blockade on Germany, one of a range of measures by which the British will wage economic warfare on the Axis powers.</dd>

-The United States launches the Neutrality Patrol.
-<dd> The United States launches the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Neutrality_Patrol" title="Neutrality Patrol">Neutrality Patrol</a>.</dd>
September 4, 1941
-USS Greer becomes the first United States warship fired upon by a German U-boat in the war, even though the United States is a neutral power. Tension heightens between the two nations as a result. The U.S. is now committed to convoy duties between the Western Hemisphere and Europe.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/USS_Greer_(DD-145)" title="USS Greer (DD-145)">USS <i>Greer</i></a> becomes the first United States warship fired upon by a German U-boat in the war, even though the United States is a neutral power. Tension heightens between the two nations as a result. The U.S. is now committed to convoy duties between the Western Hemisphere and Europe.</dd>
September 4, 1942
-Irish Republican Army riots occur in Belfast during the night.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Irish_Republican_Army" title="Irish Republican Army">Irish Republican Army</a> riots occur in Belfast during the night.</dd>
September 4, 1942
-Manhattan Engineering District is formally created, full-effort production of the atomic bomb is begun.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Manhattan_Project" title="Manhattan Project">Manhattan Engineering District</a> is formally created, full-effort production of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Atomic_bomb" title="Atomic bomb">atomic bomb</a> is begun.</dd>
September 4, 1942
-Chief of State of Vichy France Philippe Pétain and Prime Minister Pierre Laval create what will become the Service du travail obligatoire (STO).
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Head_of_state" title="Head of state">Chief of State</a> of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vichy_France" title="Vichy France">Vichy France</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Philippe_P%C3%A9tain" title="Philippe Pétain">Philippe Pétain</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_France" title="Prime Minister of France">Prime Minister</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pierre_Laval" title="Pierre Laval">Pierre Laval</a> create what will become the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Service_du_travail_obligatoire" title="Service du travail obligatoire">Service du travail obligatoire</a> (STO).</dd>
September 4, 1943
-Soviet Union declares war on Bulgaria. The 503rd Parachute Regiment under American General Douglas MacArthur lands and occupies Nadzab, just west of the port city of Lae in northeastern New Guinea. Lae falls into Australian hands and Australian troops take Salamaua.
-<dd> Soviet Union declares war on Bulgaria. The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/503rd_Infantry_Regiment_(United_States)" title="503rd Infantry Regiment (United States)">503rd Parachute Regiment</a> under American General <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Douglas_MacArthur" title="Douglas MacArthur">Douglas MacArthur</a> lands and occupies <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nadzab" title="Nadzab">Nadzab</a>, just west of the port city of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lae" title="Lae">Lae</a> in northeastern New Guinea. Lae falls into Australian hands and Australian troops take <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Salamaua" title="Salamaua">Salamaua</a>.</dd>
September 4, 1944
-A cease fire takes effect between Finland and the USSR. Operation Outward ends.
-<dd> A cease fire takes effect between Finland and the USSR. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Outward" title="Operation Outward">Operation Outward</a> ends.</dd>

September 5, 1942
-Australian and U.S. forces defeat Japanese forces at Milne Bay, Papua, the first outright defeat for Japanese land forces in the Pacific War. Their evacuation and the failure to establish an airbase eases the threat to Australia.
-<dd> Australian and U.S. forces defeat Japanese forces at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Milne_Bay" title="Battle of Milne Bay">Milne Bay</a>, Papua, the first outright defeat for Japanese land forces in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pacific_War" title="Pacific War">Pacific War</a>. Their evacuation and the failure to establish an airbase eases the threat to Australia.</dd>
September 5, 1944
-Antwerp is liberated by British 11th Armoured Division and local resistance. The uprising in Warsaw continues. United States III Corps arrives in European Theater. The Belgian, Dutch and Luxembourgish governments in exile sign the London Customs Convention, laying the foundations for the Benelux economic union.
-<dd> <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Antwerp_(city)" title="Antwerp (city)">Antwerp</a> is liberated by British 11th Armoured Division and local resistance. The uprising in Warsaw continues. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/III_Corps_(United_States)" title="III Corps (United States)">III Corps</a> arrives in European Theater. The <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgian_Government_in_Exile" title="Belgian Government in Exile">Belgian</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_government-in-exile" title="Dutch government-in-exile">Dutch</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luxembourgish_government-in-exile" title="Luxembourgish government-in-exile">Luxembourgish governments in exile</a> sign the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/London_Customs_Convention" title="London Customs Convention">London Customs Convention</a>, laying the foundations for the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Benelux" title="Benelux">Benelux economic union</a>.</dd>
September 5, 1945
-Singapore is officially liberated by British and Indian troops.
-<dd> Singapore is officially liberated by British and Indian troops.</dd>

-The German army occupies Kraków in the south of Poland; Polish army is in general retreat.

September 7, 1940
-In one of the major misjudgements of the war, the Luftwaffe shifts its focus to London, away from the RAF airfields.  Success may be measured only in the estimated 2,000 civilian dead.  Other British cities are hit. The Blitz starts

September 8, 1939
-The British Government announces the re-introduction of the convoy system for merchant ships and a full-scale blockade on German shipping.

September 8, 1941
-Siege of Leningrad begins – a reasonable date to start measuring "the 900 days." German forces begin a siege against the Soviet Union's second-largest city, Leningrad; Stalin orders the Volga Germans deported to Siberia.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Siege_of_Leningrad" title="Siege of Leningrad">Siege of Leningrad</a> begins – a reasonable date to start measuring "the 900 days." German forces begin a siege against the Soviet Union's second-largest city, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saint_Petersburg" title="Saint Petersburg">Leningrad</a>; Stalin orders the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Volga_Germans" title="Volga Germans">Volga Germans</a> deported to Siberia.</dd>
September 8, 1943
-Eisenhower publicly announces the surrender of Italy to the Allies. The Germans enact Operation Achse, the disarmament of Italian armed forces.The USAAF bombs the German General Headquarters for the Mediterranean zone at Frascati.
-<dd> Eisenhower publicly announces the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Armistice_of_Cassibile" title="Armistice of Cassibile">surrender of Italy</a> to the Allies. The Germans enact <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Achse" title="Operation Achse">Operation Achse</a>, the disarmament of Italian armed forces.The USAAF bombs the German General Headquarters for the Mediterranean zone at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frascati" title="Frascati">Frascati</a>.</dd>
September 8, 1944
-Ostend is liberated by Canadian troops. Soviet troops enter Bulgaria. The Belgian government in exile returns to Belgium from London where it has spent the war. The first successful operational use of the German V-2 rocket took place two were launched at London, and one at Paris.  A woman was killed by one that fell on the Chiswick area of London.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ostend" title="Ostend">Ostend</a> is liberated by Canadian troops. Soviet troops enter <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgaria" title="Bulgaria">Bulgaria</a>. The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgian_government_in_exile" title="Belgian government in exile">Belgian government in exile</a> returns to Belgium from London where it has spent the war. The first successful operational use of the German <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/V-2_rocket" title="V-2 rocket">V-2 rocket</a> took place: two were launched at London, and one at Paris.  A woman was killed by one that fell on the Chiswick area of London.</dd>

-The French Saar Offensive stalls at the heavily mined Warndt Forest having advanced approximately 8 miles (13 km) into lightly defended German territory.

September 9, 1940
-During the Western Desert Campaign, Italian colonial forces in Libya under General Mario Berti launch the invasion of Egypt.  The first objective is to advance from defensive positions within Libya to the border with Egypt.  Tel Aviv in the British Mandate of Palestine is bombed by Italian aircraft causing 137 deaths.
-<dd> During the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Western_Desert_Campaign" title="Western Desert Campaign">Western Desert Campaign</a>, Italian colonial forces in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a> under General <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mario_Berti" title="Mario Berti">Mario Berti</a> launch the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_invasion_of_Egypt" title="Italian invasion of Egypt">invasion of Egypt</a>.  The first objective is to advance from defensive positions within Libya to the border with <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a>. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tel_Aviv" title="Tel Aviv">Tel Aviv</a> in the British Mandate of Palestine is <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bombing_of_Palestine_in_World_War_II" title="Bombing of Palestine in World War II">bombed by Italian aircraft</a> causing 137 deaths.</dd>

September 10, 1944
-Luxembourg is liberated by U.S. First Army. Two Allied forces meet at Dijon, cutting France in half. First Allied troops enter Germany, entering Aachen, a city on the border. Dutch railway workers go on strike. The German response results in the Dutch famine of 1944.

September 11, 1939
-Viceroy of India Lord Linlithgow announces to the two houses of the Indian Legislature (the Council of State and the Legislative Assembly) that due to India's participation in the war, the plans for the Federation of India under the Government of India Act 1935 will be indefinitely postponed.
-<dd> <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Viceroy_of_India" title="Viceroy of India">Viceroy of India</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Victor_Hope,_2nd_Marquess_of_Linlithgow" title="Victor Hope, 2nd Marquess of Linlithgow">Lord Linlithgow</a> announces to the two houses of the Indian Legislature (the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Council_of_State" title="Council of State">Council of State</a> and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Legislative_Assembly" title="Legislative Assembly">Legislative Assembly</a>) that due to India's participation in the war, the plans for the Federation of India under the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Government_of_India_Act_1935" title="Government of India Act 1935">Government of India Act 1935</a> will be indefinitely postponed.</dd>

September 12, 1942
-SS commander Brandt orders 3,000–4,000 Stanislau Jews deported to the Belzec death camp on Rosh Hashana, the Jewish New Year holiday, and they were killed there that day.
-<dd> SS commander Brandt orders 3,000–4,000 Stanislau Jews deported to the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belzec_extermination_camp" title="Belzec extermination camp">Belzec death camp</a> on <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rosh_Hashana" title="Rosh Hashana">Rosh Hashana</a>, the Jewish New Year holiday, and they were killed there that day.</dd>

September 12, 1943
-Mussolini is rescued by aircraft from  mountaintop captivity by German SS troops led by Otto Skorzeny.  Mussolini is then set up by Hitler, who remains loyal to his old friend, as the head of the puppet "Italian Social Republic."
-<dd> Mussolini is rescued by aircraft from  mountaintop captivity by German SS troops led by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Otto_Skorzeny" title="Otto Skorzeny">Otto Skorzeny</a>.  Mussolini is then set up by Hitler, who remains loyal to his old friend, as the head of the puppet "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_Social_Republic" title="Italian Social Republic">Italian Social Republic</a>."</dd>

-The Second Quebec Conference (codenamed "Octagon") begins Roosevelt and Churchill discuss military cooperation in the Pacific and the future of Germany.

September 13, 1940
-After re-taking Fort Capuzzo just inside Libya, Italian colonial forces cross the border and advance into Egypt.  The Italians take the small port of Sollum, but the only resistance to the invasion is a light British screening force which withdraws as the Italians advance.
-<dd> After re-taking <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fort_Capuzzo" title="Fort Capuzzo">Fort Capuzzo</a> just inside Libya, Italian colonial forces cross the border and advance into Egypt.  The Italians take the small port of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sallum" title="Sallum">Sollum</a>, but the only resistance to the invasion is a light British screening force which withdraws as the Italians advance.</dd>

-The Battle for Stalingrad continues; it is now totally surrounded by the Germans. On the Soviet Union side General Vasily Chuikov is put in charge of the defence.

September 13, 1945
-British forces under Major-General Douglas Gracey's 20th Indian Division, some 26,000 men in all, arrive in Saigon to disarm and accept the surrender of the Japanese Occupation Forces in Vietnam south of the 16th parallel. 180,000 Chinese Nationalist soldiers, mainly poor peasants, arrive in Hanoi to disarm and accept surrender north of the line. After looting Vietnamese villages during their entire march down from China, they then proceed to loot Hanoi.
-<dd> British forces under Major-General <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Douglas_Gracey" title="Douglas Gracey">Douglas Gracey</a>'s 20th Indian Division, some 26,000 men in all, arrive in <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saigon" title="Saigon">Saigon</a> to disarm and accept the surrender of the Japanese Occupation Forces in Vietnam south of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/16th_parallel_north" title="16th parallel north">16th parallel</a>. 180,000 Chinese Nationalist soldiers, mainly poor peasants, arrive in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hanoi" title="Hanoi">Hanoi</a> to disarm and accept surrender north of the line. After looting Vietnamese villages during their entire march down from China, they then proceed to loot Hanoi.</dd>
September 14, 1939
-Destroyers escorting the aircraft carrier HMS Ark Royal sank the U-39 with depth charges. All crew members were rescued and taken prisoner. It was the first sinking of a German U-boat in WWII.
-<dd> Destroyers escorting the aircraft carrier <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HMS_Ark_Royal_(91)" title="HMS Ark Royal (91)">HMS <i>Ark Royal</i></a> sank the <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_submarine_U-39_(1938)" title="German submarine U-39 (1938)">U-39</a></i> with <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Depth_charge" title="Depth charge">depth charges</a>. All crew members were rescued and taken prisoner. It was the first sinking of a German U-boat in WWII.</dd>

September 15, 1941
-"Self-government" of Estonia, headed by Hjalmar Mäe, is appointed by German military administration. "Moving Aktion" in Vilna Ghetto. Of 3,500 Jews "moved" between ghetto sections, only 550 arrive. The remaining 2,950 Jews are shot at the Ponary massacre death site.
-<dd> "Self-government" of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Estonia" title="Estonia">Estonia</a>, headed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hjalmar_M%C3%A4e" title="Hjalmar Mäe">Hjalmar Mäe</a>, is appointed by German military administration. "Moving Aktion" in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vilna_Ghetto" title="Vilna Ghetto">Vilna Ghetto</a>. Of 3,500 Jews "moved" between ghetto sections, only 550 arrive. The remaining 2,950 Jews are shot at the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ponary_massacre" title="Ponary massacre">Ponary massacre</a> death site.</dd>
September 15, 1942
