September 15, 1942
-Light carrier USS Wasp is sunk by a Japanese submarine off Guadalcanal./dd>18 Battle of the "grain silo" in Stalingrad; the Germans are beaten back. The Red Army begins ferrying troops across the Volga at night.19 Allied attack on Jalo, Libya is repulsed by Germans.20 RAF bombs Munich and Saarbrücken.20 The Greek Panhellenic Union of Fighting Youths blows up the offices of the pro-Nazi National-Socialist Patriotic Organisation in central Athens, thwarting attempts to raise a Greek volunteer legion for the Eastern Front.23 General Rommel leaves North Africa for medical treatment in Germany.23–27 In the Third Battle of Matanikau River, Guadalcanal, Japanese naval bombardment and landing forces nearly destroy Henderson Field in an attempt to take it, but the land forces are soon driven back.24 United States of America deploys the I Corps to the Pacific Theater.28 The Japanese continue their retreat back down the Kokoda Track in New Guinea.30 The Eagle Squadron (American volunteers in the RAF) are officially transferred to the US Army Air Force.30 Hitler speaks to the nation and boasts that Stalingrad will be taken.
-<dd> Light carrier <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/USS_Wasp_(CV-7)" title="USS Wasp (CV-7)">USS <i>Wasp</i></a> is sunk by a Japanese submarine off Guadalcanal./dd&gt;<dd>18: Battle of the "grain silo" in Stalingrad; the Germans are beaten back. The Red Army begins ferrying troops across the Volga at night.</dd><dd>19: Allied attack on <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jalu" title="Jalu">Jalo</a>, Libya is repulsed by Germans.</dd><dd>20: RAF bombs <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Munich" title="Munich">Munich</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saarbr%C3%BCcken" title="Saarbrücken">Saarbrücken</a>.</dd><dd>20: The Greek <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Panhellenic_Union_of_Fighting_Youths" title="Panhellenic Union of Fighting Youths">Panhellenic Union of Fighting Youths</a> blows up the offices of the pro-Nazi <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/National-Socialist_Patriotic_Organisation" title="National-Socialist Patriotic Organisation">National-Socialist Patriotic Organisation</a> in central <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Athens" title="Athens">Athens</a>, thwarting attempts to raise a Greek volunteer legion for the Eastern Front.</dd><dd>23: General Rommel leaves North Africa for medical treatment in Germany.</dd><dd>23–27: In the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Actions_along_the_Matanikau" September 16, 1940
-Selective Training and Service Act of 1940 introduces the first peacetime conscription (this time for men between 21 and 35) in United States history. The Italian invasion of Egypt comes to a halt when approximately five Italian divisions set up defensively in a series of armed camps after advancing about 95 km (59 mi) to Sidi Barrani.  The Italians never approach the main British positions at Mersa Matruh.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Selective_Training_and_Service_Act_of_1940" title="Selective Training and Service Act of 1940">Selective Training and Service Act of 1940</a> introduces the first peacetime <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Conscription" title="Conscription">conscription</a> (this time for men between 21 and 35) in United States history. The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_invasion_of_Egypt" title="Italian invasion of Egypt">Italian invasion of Egypt</a> comes to a halt when approximately five Italian divisions set up defensively in a series of armed camps after advancing about 95 km (59 mi) to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sidi_Barrani" title="Sidi Barrani">Sidi Barrani</a>.  The Italians never approach the main British positions at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mersa_Matruh" title="Mersa Matruh">Mersa Matruh</a>.</dd>

September 18, 1939
-Polish President Ignacy Mościcki and Commander-in-Chief Edward Rydz-Śmigły leave Poland for Romania, where they are both interned; Russian forces reach Vilnius and Brest-Litovsk. Polish submarine escapes from Tallinn; Estonia's neutrality is questioned by the Soviet Union and Germany.
-<dd> Polish President <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ignacy_Mo%C5%9Bcicki" title="Ignacy Mościcki">Ignacy Mościcki</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Commander-in-Chief" title="Commander-in-Chief">Commander-in-Chief</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Rydz-%C5%9Amig%C5%82y" title="Edward Rydz-Śmigły">Edward Rydz-Śmigły</a> leave Poland for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Romania" title="Romania">Romania</a>, where they are both interned; Russian forces reach <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vilnius" title="Vilnius">Vilnius</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brest-Litovsk" title="Brest-Litovsk">Brest-Litovsk</a>. Polish submarine escapes from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tallinn" title="Tallinn">Tallinn</a>; <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Estonia" title="Estonia">Estonia</a>'s neutrality is questioned by the Soviet Union and Germany.</dd>

September 20, 1939
-German submarine U-27 is sunk with depth charges from the British destroyers HMS Fortune and HMS Forester.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/U-boat" title="U-boat">German submarine</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_submarine_U-27_(1936)" title="German submarine U-27 (1936)"><i>U-27</i></a> is sunk with depth charges from the British destroyers <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HMS_Fortune_(H70)" title="HMS Fortune (H70)">HMS <i>Fortune</i></a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HMS_Forester_(H74)" title="HMS Forester (H74)">HMS <i>Forester</i></a>.</dd>

September 21, 1939
-Romanian Prime Minister Armand Călinescu is assassinated by the Iron Guard, an ultra-nationalistic group in Romania.

September 21, 1943
-The battle of the Solomons can now be considered at an unofficial end. The Massacre of the Acqui Division begins After resisting for a week, the Italian Acqui division on the Greek island of Cephallonia surrenders to the Germans. During the next days, over 4,500 Italians are executed and a further 3,000 are lost during transport at sea.
-<dd> The battle of the Solomons can now be considered at an unofficial end. The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Massacre_of_the_Acqui_Division" title="Massacre of the Acqui Division">Massacre of the Acqui Division</a> begins: After resisting for a week, the Italian <i>Acqui</i> division on the Greek island of Cephallonia surrenders to the Germans. During the next days, over 4,500 Italians are executed and a further 3,000 are lost during transport at sea.</dd>
September 21, 1944
-British forces take Rimini, Italy. The Second Dumbarton Oaks Conference begins it will set guidelines for the United Nations. In Belgium, Charles of Flanders is sworn in as Prince-Regent while a decision is delayed about whether King Leopold III can ever return to his functions after being accused of collaboration. San Marino declares war on the Axis. The Government of Estonia prints a few hundred copies of the Riigi Teataja (State Gazette) and is forced to flee under Soviet pressure.
-<dd> British forces take <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rimini" title="Rimini">Rimini</a>, Italy. The Second Dumbarton Oaks Conference begins: it will set guidelines for the United Nations. In Belgium, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Prince_Charles,_Count_of_Flanders" title="Prince Charles, Count of Flanders">Charles of Flanders</a> is sworn in as Prince-Regent while a decision is delayed about whether <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Leopold_III_of_Belgium" title="Leopold III of Belgium">King Leopold III</a> can ever return to his functions after being accused of collaboration. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/San_Marino" title="San Marino">San Marino</a> declares war on the Axis. The Government of Estonia prints a few hundred copies of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Riigi_Teataja" title="Riigi Teataja">Riigi Teataja</a> (State Gazette) and is forced to flee under Soviet pressure.</dd>

September 22, 1943
-Australian forces land at Finschhafen, a small port in New Guinea. The Japanese continue the battle well into October. British midget submarines attack the German battleship Tirpitz, at anchor in a Norwegian fjord, crippling her for six months.
-<dd> Australian forces land at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Finschhafen" title="Finschhafen">Finschhafen</a>, a small port in New Guinea. September 22, 1944
-The Red Army takes Tallinn, the first Baltic harbour outside the minefields of the Gulf of Finland. The Germans surrender at Boulogne.
-<dd> The Red Army takes <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tallinn" title="Tallinn">Tallinn</a>, the first <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Baltic_Sea" title="Baltic Sea">Baltic</a> harbour outside the minefields of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gulf_of_Finland" title="Gulf of Finland">Gulf of Finland</a>. The Germans surrender at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Boulogne-sur-Mer" title="Boulogne-sur-Mer">Boulogne</a>.</dd>
September 22, 1945
-The British rearm 1,400 French soldiers from Japanese internment camps around Saigon. In Saigon, on the night of 24 September, a mob composed of Viet-Minh militants and sympathizers attacks French colonial administration and kills around 150 European civilians. An estimated 20,000 French civilians live in Saigon.

September 25, 1944
-British troops pull out of Arnhem with the failure of Operation Market Garden. Over 6,000 paratroopers are captured; of the British 1st Airbourne Division, just under 8,000 of the 10,005 paratroopers are declared casualties, a staggering 80% loss. Hopes of an early end to the war are now abandoned. United States IX Corps arrives in Pacific Theater.

October 1, 1941
-Majdanek concentration camp (German Konzentrationslager Lublin) and later to become extermination camp is opened. Vilna Ghetto Yom Kippur Aktions (German annihilation operations) begin. -<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Majdanek_concentration_camp" title="Majdanek concentration camp">Majdanek concentration camp</a> (German: Konzentrationslager <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lublin" title="Lublin">Lublin</a>) and later to become <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Extermination_camp" title="Extermination camp">extermination camp</a> is opened. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vilna_Ghetto" title="Vilna Ghetto">Vilna Ghetto</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yom_Kippur" title="Yom Kippur">Yom Kippur</a> Aktions (German annihilation operations) begin. In four separate incidents 3,900 Jews are kidnapped, shot and killed at the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ponary_massacre" title="Ponary massacre">Ponary massacre</a> death site, continued with an additional 2,000 Jews kidnapped and killed there, in the next two days.</dd>

October 1, 1944
-A Hungarian delegation arrives in Moscow to negotiate an armistice with the USSR. Soviet troops enter Yugoslavia.
-<dd> A Hungarian delegation arrives in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moscow" title="Moscow">Moscow</a> to negotiate an armistice with the USSR. Soviet troops enter <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yugoslavia" title="Yugoslavia">Yugoslavia</a>.</dd>
October 1, 1945
-In Southern Vietnam, a purely bilateral British/French agreement recognizes French administration of the southern zone. In northern Vietnam, Chinese troops go on a "rampage". Hồ's Việt Minh are hopelessly ill-equipped to deal with it.
-<dd> In <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southern_Vietnam" title="Southern Vietnam">Southern Vietnam</a>, a purely bilateral British/French agreement recognizes French administration of the southern zone. In <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Northern_Vietnam" title="Northern Vietnam">northern Vietnam</a>, Chinese troops go on a "rampage". <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/H%E1%BB%93_Ch%C3%AD_Minh" title="Hồ Chí Minh">Hồ</a>'s Việt Minh are hopelessly ill-equipped to deal with it.</dd>
October 1, 1945
-[1-30] The non fraternization directive for U.S. troops against German civilians was rescinded. Previously even speaking to a German could lead to court martial, except for "small children", these had been exempt in June 1945.
-<dd> The non fraternization directive for U.S. troops against German civilians was rescinded. Previously even speaking to a German could lead to court martial, except for "small children", these had been exempt in June 1945.</dd>
October 2, 1939
-Declaration of Panama is approved by American Republics. Belligerent activities should not take place within waters adjacent to the American continent. A neutrality zone of some 300 miles (480 km) in breadth is to be patrolled by the U.S. Navy.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pan-American_Security_Zone" title="Pan-American Security Zone">Declaration of Panama</a> is approved by American Republics. Belligerent activities should not take place within waters adjacent to the American continent. A neutrality zone of some 300 miles (480 km) in breadth is to be patrolled by the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/U.S._Navy" title="U.S. Navy">U.S. Navy</a>.</dd>
October 2, 1940
-The bombing of London continues throughout the month.
-<dd> The <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bombing_of_London" title="Bombing of London">bombing of London</a> continues throughout the month.</dd>
October 2, 1941
-Operation Typhoon – German "Central" forces begin an all-out offensive against Moscow. Leading the defense of the capital is General Georgi Zhukov, already a Hero of Soviet Union for his command in the conflict against the Japanese in the Russian Far East and at Leningrad.
-<dd> <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Typhoon" title="Operation Typhoon">Operation Typhoon</a> – German "Central" forces begin an all-out offensive against Moscow. Leading the defense of the capital is General Georgi Zhukov, already a Hero of Soviet Union for his command in the conflict against the Japanese in the Russian Far East and at Leningrad.</dd>
October 2, 1944
-Germans finally succeed in putting down the Warsaw Uprising by the Polish Home Army. American troops are now in a full-scale attack on the German "West Wall". Allied forces land on Crete.
-<dd> Germans finally succeed in putting down the Warsaw Uprising by the Polish <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Home_Army" title="Home Army">Home Army</a>. American troops are now in a full-scale attack on the German "West Wall". Allied forces land on <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Crete" title="Crete">Crete</a>.</dd>
October 3, 1939
-British forces move to the Belgian border, anticipating a German invasion of the West.
-<dd> British forces move to the Belgian border, anticipating a German invasion of the West.</dd>
October 3, 1939
-Lithuanians meet Stalin and Molotov in Moscow. Stalin offers Lithuania the city of Vilnius (in Poland) in return for allowing Soviet military bases in Lithuania. The Lithuanians are reluctant.
-<dd> Lithuanians meet <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_Stalin" title="Joseph Stalin">Stalin</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vyacheslav_Molotov" title="Vyacheslav Molotov">Molotov</a> in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moscow" title="Moscow">Moscow</a>. Stalin offers <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuania" title="Lithuania">Lithuania</a> the city of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vilnius" title="Vilnius">Vilnius</a> (in Poland) in return for allowing Soviet military bases in Lithuania. The Lithuanians are reluctant.</dd>
October 3, 1940
-Warsaw's Jews are directed to move into the Warsaw ghetto.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Warsaw" title="Warsaw">Warsaw</a>'s Jews are directed to move into the Warsaw ghetto.</dd>
October 3, 1941
-Mahatma Gandhi urges his followers to begin a passive resistance against British rule in India.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mahatma_Gandhi" title="Mahatma Gandhi">Mahatma Gandhi</a> urges his followers to begin a passive resistance against British rule in India.</dd>
October 3, 1942
-First successful launch of A4-rocket at Peenemünde, Germany. The rocket flies 147 kilometres wide and reaches a height of 84.5 kilometres and is therefore the first man-made object reaching space.
-<dd> First successful launch of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/V-2_rocket" title="V-2 rocket">A4-rocket</a> at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Peenem%C3%BCnde" title="Peenemünde">Peenemünde</a>, Germany. The rocket flies 147 kilometres wide and reaches a height of 84.5 kilometres and is therefore the first man-made object reaching space.</dd>
October 3, 1943
-Churchill appoints Lord Louis Mountbatten the commander of South East Asia Command.
-<dd> Churchill appoints <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Louis_Mountbatten,_1st_Earl_Mountbatten_of_Burma" title="Louis Mountbatten, 1st Earl Mountbatten of Burma">Lord Louis Mountbatten</a> the commander of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/South-East_Asian_theatre_of_World_War_II#Allied_command_structure" title="South-East Asian theatre of World War II">South East Asia Command</a>.</dd>

-Adolf Hitler and Benito Mussolini meet at the Brenner Pass to discuss the prospects in the war.

October 5, 1939
-Latvia signs a 10-year Mutual Assistance Pact with the Soviet Union, which allows the Soviets to have 25,000 men in military bases in Latvia. Stalin promises to respect Latvian independence.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvia" title="Latvia">Latvia</a> signs a <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Soviet-Latvian_Mutual_Assistance_Treaty" title="Soviet-Latvian Mutual Assistance Treaty">10-year Mutual Assistance Pact</a> with the Soviet Union, which allows the Soviets to have 25,000 men in military bases in Latvia. Stalin promises to respect Latvian independence.</dd>

October 6, 1939
-Chinese army reportedly defeats the Japanese at the Battle of Changsha.

October 6, 1939
-Polish resistance in the Polish September Campaign comes to an end. Hitler speaks before the Reichstag, declaring a desire for a conference with Britain and France to restore peace.
-<dd> Polish resistance in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Invasion_of_Poland" title="Invasion of Poland">Polish September Campaign</a> comes to an end. <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hitler" title="Hitler">Hitler</a> speaks before the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Reichstag_(Weimar_Republic)" title="Reichstag (Weimar Republic)">Reichstag</a>, declaring a desire for a conference with Britain and France to restore peace.</dd>
October 6, 1942
-By mutual arrangement, the Allies agree on a strategy whereby Americans will bomb in the daytime and the RAF at night.
-<dd> By mutual arrangement, the Allies agree on a strategy whereby Americans will bomb in the daytime and the RAF at night.</dd>
October 6, 1943
-The Naval Battle of Vella Lavella completes the second phase of Operation Cartwheel.
-<dd> The <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Naval_Battle_of_Vella_Lavella" title="Naval Battle of Vella Lavella">Naval Battle of Vella Lavella</a> completes the second phase of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Cartwheel" title="Operation Cartwheel">Operation Cartwheel</a>.</dd>
October 6, 1944
-Soviet and Czechoslovak troops enter northeastern Slovakia. The Battle of Debrecen begins as German and Soviet forces advance against each other in eastern Hungary.
-<dd> Soviet and Czechoslovak troops enter northeastern <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovakia" title="Slovakia">Slovakia</a>. The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Debrecen" title="Battle of Debrecen">Battle of Debrecen</a> begins as German and Soviet forces advance against each other in eastern Hungary.</dd>
October 7, 1940
-Responding to a Romanian request made on 7 September, Germany deploys a military mission to Romania to provide training for the Romanian Army and guard the Romanian oilfields.

-98 American civilian prisoners were executed on Wake Island.

October 7, 1944
-A riot took place at Auschwitz concentration camp when the Sonderkommando Jewish collaborators came to understand that they also were slated for extermination.  Over 450 were killed in suppressing the revolt, along with many others who escaped the camp in the melee.
-<dd> A riot took place at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Auschwitz_concentration_camp" title="Auschwitz concentration camp">Auschwitz concentration camp</a> when the Sonderkommando Jewish collaborators came to understand that they also were slated for extermination.  Over 450 were killed in suppressing the revolt, along with many others who escaped the camp in the melee.</dd>
October 8, 1941
-In their invasion of the southern Soviet Union, Germany reaches the Sea of Azov with the capture of Mariupol. However, there are signs that the invasion is beginning to bog down as rainy weather creates muddy roads for both tanks and men.
-<dd> In their invasion of the southern Soviet Union, Germany reaches the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sea_of_Azov" title="Sea of Azov">Sea of Azov</a> with the capture of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mariupol" title="Mariupol">Mariupol</a>. However, there are signs that the invasion is beginning to bog down as rainy weather creates muddy roads for both tanks and men.</dd>

-Germany issues orders (Case Yellow) to prepare for the invasion of Belgium, France, Luxembourg, and the Netherlands.

October 10, 1939
-Lithuania signs a 15-year Mutual Assistance Pact with the Soviet Union, which allows the Soviets to have 20,000 men in military bases in Lithuania. In a secret protocol, Vilnius is made Lithuanian territory.
-<dd> Lithuania signs a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Soviet%E2%80%93Lithuanian_Mutual_Assistance_Treaty" title="Soviet–Lithuanian Mutual Assistance Treaty">15-year Mutual Assistance Pact</a> with the Soviet Union, which allows the Soviets to have 20,000 men in military bases in Lithuania. In a secret protocol, Vilnius is made Lithuanian territory.</dd>

October 12, 1941
-HMS Ark Royal delivers a squadron of Hurricane fighter planes to Malta. Bloody Sunday massacre at Stanisławów, 8,000–12,000 Jews were rounded up and shot into pits by SIPO (Ukrainian police) together with German uniformed SS men. Dr. Tenenbaum of the Judenrat heroically refuses the offer of exemption and is shot along with the others.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HMS_Ark_Royal_(91)" title="HMS Ark Royal (91)">HMS <i>Ark Royal</i></a> delivers a squadron of Hurricane fighter planes to Malta. <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stanis%C5%82aw%C3%B3w_Ghetto#Bloody_Sunday_massacre" title="Stanisławów Ghetto">Bloody Sunday massacre</a></i> at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stanis%C5%82aw%C3%B3w_Ghetto" title="Stanisławów Ghetto">Stanisławów</a>, 8,000–12,000 Jews were rounded up and shot into pits by SIPO (<a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainische_Hilfspolizei" title="Ukrainische Hilfspolizei">Ukrainian police</a>) together with German uniformed SS men. Dr. Tenenbaum of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Judenrat" title="Judenrat">Judenrat</a> heroically refuses the offer of exemption and is shot along with the others.</dd>

October 14, 1943
-229 of 292 B-17s reached the target in the Second Raid on Schweinfurt. Losses are so heavy that the long range daylight bombing campaign is suspended until the bombers can be escorted by P-51 fighters.Members of the Sobibor extermination camp underground, led by Polish-Jewish prisoner Leon Feldhendler and Soviet-Jewish POW Alexander Pechersky, succeeded in covertly killing eleven German SS officers and a number of camp guards. Although their plan was to kill all the SS and walk out of the main gate of the camp, the killings were discovered and the inmates ran for their lives under fire. About 300 out of the 600 prisoners in the camp escaped into the forests.
-<dd> 229 of 292 <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/B-17_Flying_Fortress" title="B-17 Flying Fortress">B-17s</a> reached the target in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Second_Raid_on_Schweinfurt" title="Second Raid on Schweinfurt">Second Raid on Schweinfurt</a>. Losses are so heavy that the long range daylight bombing campaign is suspended until the bombers can be escorted by P-51 fighters.Members of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sobibor_extermination_camp" title="Sobibor extermination camp">Sobibor extermination camp</a> underground, led by Polish-Jewish prisoner <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Leon_Feldhendler" title="Leon Feldhendler">Leon Feldhendler</a> and Soviet-Jewish POW <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alexander_Pechersky" title="Alexander Pechersky">Alexander Pechersky</a>, succeeded in covertly killing eleven German SS officers and a number of camp guards. Although their plan was to kill all the SS and walk out of the main gate of the camp, the killings were discovered and the inmates ran for their lives under fire. About 300 out of the 600 prisoners in the camp escaped into the forests.</dd>

October 22, 1941
-Odessa massacre begins and continues for two days. 25,000 to 34,000 Jews are led in a long procession and are shot and killed in an antitank ditch, or burnt alive after being crowded into four buildings.  The massacre began after, that day, a delayed bomb planted by the Soviets kills 67 people at the Romanian headquarters, including the Romanian commander General Glogojeanu. 35,000 Jews are expelled to the Slobodka Ghetto and are left in freezing conditions for 10 days. Many perish in the cold.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/1941_Odessa_massacre" title="1941 Odessa massacre">Odessa massacre</a> begins and continues for two days. 25,000 to 34,000 Jews are led in a long procession and are shot and killed in an antitank ditch, or burnt alive after being crowded into four buildings. The massacre began after, that day, a delayed bomb planted by the Soviets kills 67 people at the Romanian headquarters, including the Romanian commander General Glogojeanu. 35,000 Jews are expelled to the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vilijampol%C4%97" title="Vilijampolė">Slobodka</a> Ghetto and are left in freezing conditions for 10 days. Many perish in the cold.</dd>

-<dd> German <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Army_Group_South" title="Army Group South">Army Group South</a> forces reach <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sevastopol" title="Sevastopol">Sevastopol</a> in the Crimea, but the tanks of the "Northern" forces are slowed or stopped entirely by mud.</dd>
October 27, 1944
-The Battle of Hürtgen Forest is developing. It will continue through October and November and have its last attacks in December.
-<dd> The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_H%C3%BCrtgen_Forest" title="Battle of Hürtgen Forest">Battle of Hürtgen Forest</a> is developing. It will continue through October and November and have its last attacks in December.</dd>
October 28, 1940
-At about 0300 am the Italian ambassador to Greece issues ultimatum to Greece and Greek Prime Minister Metaxas replies  "So it is war".  The Italian Royal Army launches attacks into Greece from Italian-held Albania and begins the Greco-Italian War. Hitler is angered at the initiative of his ally.
-<dd> At about 03:00 am the Italian ambassador to Greece issues ultimatum to Greece and Greek Prime Minister <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ioannis_Metaxas" title="Ioannis Metaxas">Metaxas</a> replies:  "So it is war".  The <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_Royal_Army" title="Italian Royal Army">Italian Royal Army</a> launches attacks into Greece from <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albania_under_Italy" title="Albania under Italy">Italian-held Albania</a> and begins the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greco-Italian_War" title="Greco-Italian War">Greco-Italian War</a>. Hitler is angered at the initiative of his ally.</dd>
October 28, 1941
-Bolekhiv first aktion massacre – 1,000 of the leading Jews rounded up by list, tortured, and on the following day 800 of the surviving Jews, were shot or buried alive at a nearby forest. The re-discovered atrocities and testimony in 1996 lead to Patrick Desbois's research on the German method of "One Bullet, One Jew" extermination in 1941 and 1942.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Holocaust_in_Bolekhiv" title="Holocaust in Bolekhiv">Bolekhiv first <i>aktion</i> massacre</a> – 1,000 of the leading Jews rounded up by list, tortured, and on the following day 800 of the surviving Jews, were shot or buried alive at a nearby forest. The re-discovered atrocities and testimony in 1996 lead to Patrick Desbois's research on the German method of "One Bullet, One Jew" extermination in 1941 and 1942.</dd>
October 29, 1940
-Very heavy convoy losses during this period as numbers of U-boats increase.
-<dd> Very heavy convoy losses during this period as numbers of U-boats increase.</dd>

-The first number drawings for US Selective Service Act draftees.
-<dd> The first number drawings for US <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Selective_Training_and_Service_Act_of_1940" title="Selective Training and Service Act of 1940">Selective Service Act</a> draftees.</dd>

-Vilna Ghetto II liquidated. 2,500 Jews killed.

-The Japanese continue to send troops as reinforcements into Guadalcanal.

October 30, 1945
-[1-30] The non fraternization directive for U.S. troops against German civilians was rescinded. Previously even speaking to a German could lead to court martial, except for "small children", these had been exempt in June 1945.
-<dd> The non fraternization directive for U.S. troops against German civilians was rescinded. Previously even speaking to a German could lead to court martial, except for "small children", these had been exempt in June 1945.</dd>
November 1, 1939
-Parts of Poland, including the Danzig Corridor, are annexed by Germany.	Soviet Union annexes the eastern parts of occupied Poland to Ukraine and Belorussia.
-<dd> Parts of Poland, including the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danzig_Corridor" title="Danzig Corridor">Danzig Corridor</a>, are annexed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nazi_Germany" title="Nazi Germany">Germany</a>.	<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet Union</a> annexes the eastern parts of occupied Poland to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_Soviet_Socialist_Republic" title="Ukrainian Soviet Socialist Republic">Ukraine</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Byelorussian_Soviet_Socialist_Republic" title="Byelorussian Soviet Socialist Republic">Belorussia</a>.</dd>
November 1, 1940
-Turkey declared neutrality in the Italo-Greek war.
-<dd> Turkey declared neutrality in the Italo-Greek war.</dd>
November 1, 1941
-President Franklin D. Roosevelt announces that the U.S. Coast Guard will now be under the direction of the U.S. Navy, a transition of authority usually reserved only for wartime.

November 1, 1943
-In Operation Goodtime, United States Marines land on Bougainville in the Solomon Islands.  The fighting on this island will continue to the end of the war.
-<dd> In <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Goodtime" title="Operation Goodtime">Operation Goodtime</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States_Marines" title="United States Marines">United States Marines</a> land on Bougainville in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Solomon_Islands" title="Solomon Islands">Solomon Islands</a>.  The fighting on this island will continue to the end of the war.</dd>
November 1, 1944
-British forces occupy Salonika, Greece, and distribute food in Athens, which is experiencing famine. "Operation Infatuate", an Allied attempt to free the approaches to Antwerp begins; amphibious landings take place on Walcheren Island.
-<dd> British forces occupy <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thessaloniki" title="Thessaloniki">Salonika</a>, Greece, and distribute food in Athens, which is experiencing famine. "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Infatuate" title="Operation Infatuate">Operation Infatuate</a>", an Allied attempt to free the approaches to Antwerp begins; amphibious landings take place on <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Walcheren" title="Walcheren">Walcheren</a> Island.</dd>
November 2, 1940
-The Italian advance into Greece continues.  Vovousa is captured and Italian aircraft bomb Salonika.

November 2, 1941
-Political conflict in Yugoslavia as leftists under Tito (Josip Broz) are in competition with the more conservative Serbs under Draža Mihailović.

November 2, 1943
-In the early morning hours, American and Japanese ships fight the inconclusive Battle of Empress Augusta Bay off Bougainville, but the Japanese are unable to land reinforcements. British troops, in Italy, reach the Garigliano River.
-<dd> In the early morning hours, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" title="United States">American</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japanese</a> ships fight the inconclusive <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Empress_Augusta_Bay" title="Battle of Empress Augusta Bay">Battle of Empress Augusta Bay</a> off Bougainville, but the Japanese are unable to land reinforcements. British troops, in Italy, reach the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Garigliano_River" title="Garigliano River">Garigliano River</a>.</dd>
November 2, 1944
-Canadian troops take Zeebrugge in Belgium; Belgium is now entirely liberated.

-Finland and Soviet Union again negotiate new borders. Finns mistrust Stalin's aims and refuse to give up territory breaking their defensive line.

-Germans take Kursk. Vilna Ghetto Gelbschein III Aktion. 1,200 Jews killed.

-Second Battle of El Alamein ends - German forces under Erwin Rommel are forced to retreat during the night.

November 4, 1939
-The U.S. Neutrality Act is passed the French and British may buy arms, but on a strictly cash basis. American isolationists find the act an "outrage."

November 4, 1939
-A German physicist working at Siemens AG sends an anonymous letter to the British Embassy in Oslo offering Britain a report on present and future German weapons technologies.

-[1-4] The Americans begin the Matanikau Offensive against the Japanese

November 4, 1944
-Remaining Axis forces withdraw from the Greek mainland. German occupation forces will remain in several Greek islands until capitulation.
-<dd> Remaining Axis forces withdraw from the Greek mainland. German occupation forces will remain in several Greek islands until capitulation.</dd>
November 4, 1944
-British Gen. John Dill dies in Washington, D.C., and is buried in Arlington National Cemetery, the only foreigner to be so honored at the time.
-<dd> British Gen. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Dill" title="John Dill">John Dill</a> dies in Washington, D.C., and is buried in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arlington_National_Cemetery" title="Arlington National Cemetery">Arlington National Cemetery</a>, the only foreigner to be so honored at the time.</dd>
November 5, 1940
-President Roosevelt wins a third term. The British see the event as promising of more help from the US.
-<dd> President Roosevelt wins a third term. The British see the event as promising of more help from the US.</dd>
November 5, 1940
-HMS Jervis Bay, a merchant cruiser, is sunk on convoy duty, but much of the convoy escapes. The loss becomes a media event.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HMS_Jervis_Bay" title="HMS Jervis Bay">HMS <i>Jervis Bay</i></a>, a merchant cruiser, is sunk on convoy duty, but much of the convoy escapes. The loss becomes a media event.</dd>
November 5, 1942
-German III Panzer Corps and Romanian 2nd Mountain Division capture the town of Alagir, which is the furthest south the Axis would reach on the Eastern Front.
-<dd> German <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/III_Army_Corps_(Wehrmacht)" title="III Army Corps (Wehrmacht)">III Panzer Corps</a> and Romanian 2nd Mountain Division capture the town of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alagir" title="Alagir">Alagir</a>, which is the furthest south the Axis would reach on the Eastern Front.</dd>
November 5, 1943
-The Italians bomb the Vatican in a failed attempt to knock out the Vatican radio.
-<dd> The Italians <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bombing_of_the_Vatican" title="Bombing of the Vatican">bomb the Vatican</a> in a failed attempt to knock out the Vatican radio.</dd>
November 5, 1944
-US planes bomb Singapore. The aircraft carrier USS Lexington is heavily damaged by kamikaze attacks.
-<dd> US planes bomb <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Singapore" title="Singapore">Singapore</a>. The aircraft carrier USS Lexington is heavily damaged by kamikaze attacks.</dd>
November 6, 1941
-Soviet leader Joseph Stalin addresses the Soviet Union for only the second time during his three-decade rule (the first time was earlier that year on July 2). He states that even though 350,000 troops were killed in German attacks so far, that the Germans have lost 4.5 million soldiers (a gross exaggeration) and that Soviet victory was near.
-<dd> Soviet leader <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_Stalin" title="Joseph Stalin">Joseph Stalin</a> addresses the Soviet Union for only the second time during his three-decade rule (the first time was earlier that year on July 2). He states that even though 350,000 troops were killed in German attacks so far, that the Germans have lost 4.5 million soldiers (a gross exaggeration) and that Soviet victory was near.</dd>

-Carlson's Patrol begins.

November 8, 1939
-Hitler escapes a bomb blast in a Munich beerhall, where he was speaking on the anniversary of the Beer Hall Putsch of 1923. British bombers coincidentally bomb Munich.
-<dd> Hitler escapes a bomb blast in a Munich beerhall, where he was speaking on the anniversary of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beer_Hall_Putsch" title="Beer Hall Putsch">Beer Hall Putsch</a> of 1923. British bombers coincidentally bomb Munich.</dd>
November 8, 1940
-The Battle of Elaia–Kalamas ends and the Italians end their futile offensive in Greece.
-<dd> The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Elaia%E2%80%93Kalamas" title="Battle of Elaia–Kalamas">Battle of Elaia–Kalamas</a> ends and the Italians end their futile offensive in Greece.</dd>
November 8, 1942
-Operation Torch, the Allied invasion of Vichy-controlled Morocco and Algeria, begins.8-16 French resistance coup in Algiers, consisting of about 400 fighters neutralise the Vichyist XIXth Army Corps and the Vichyist generals (Juin, Darlan, etc.), contributing significantly to the immediate success of the operation.8 The United States Combat Command "B" of the 1st Armored Division lands east and west of Oran as part of Operation Torch.10 In violation of a 1940 armistice, Germany invades Vichy France; they are responding to the fact that French Admiral François Darlan has signed an armistice with the Allies in North Africa.10 Oran, Algeria falls to US troops; 17 French ships are sunk at Oran, causing a rift between the French and the Allies. There are more Allied landings near the Tunisian border.10 Montgomery begins a major British offensive beginning at Sollum on the Libya/Egypt border. The British reach Bardia on the 11th, Tobruk on the 12th, and Benghazi on the 18th.10 Lieutenant General Montgomery is knighted and made a full General.10 Churchill speaks "This is not the end. It is not even the beginning of the end. But it is, perhaps, the end of the beginning."11 Convoys reach Malta from Alexandria; an official announcement proclaims that the island is "relieved of its siege".12 Battle of Guadalcanal - A climactic naval battle near Guadalcanal starts between Japanese and American naval forces.12 The Red Army makes an attempt to relieve Stalingrad at Kotelnikov.13 British Eighth Army recaptures Tobruk.13 Battle of Guadalcanal aviators from USS Enterprise sink the Japanese battleship Hiei. Notably, USS Juneau is sunk with much of its crew, including the five Sullivan brothers.14 USS Washington attacks the Japanese battleship Kirishima; the Japanese ship would capsize at 0325 on the morning of 15 November.15 The naval battle of Guadalcanal ends. Although the United States Navy suffers heavy losses, it still retains control of the sea around Guadalcanal.15 The British move westward in Tunisia.16 British Eighth Army recaptures Derna.17 Japanese send reinforcements into New Guinea; Americans are stymied at Buna.18 Heavy British RAF raid on Berlin with few losses.19 At Stalingrad the Soviet Union forces under General Georgy Zhukov launch Operation Uranus aimed at encircling the Germans in the city and thus turning the tide of battle in the USSR's favor.20 The Allies take Benghazi, Libya; the Afrika Corps continues the retreat westward.21 The Red Army attempt at encirclement of Stalingrad continues with obvious success.21 American army moves to shove Japanese off the extreme western end of Guadalcanal.22 Battle of Stalingrad The situation for the German attackers of Stalingrad seems desperate during the Soviet counter-attack; General Friedrich Paulus sends Adolf Hitler a telegram saying that the German 6th Army is surrounded.22 Red Army troops complete the encirclement of the Germans at Kalach, west of Stalingrad.23 "Der Kessel"-- the Cauldron, a description of the heavy fighting at Stalingrad; Hitler orders General Paulus not to retreat, at any cost.25 The encirclement of Stalingrad continues to stabilise. Hitler reiterates his demand of Paulus not to surrender.25 Operation Harling a team of British SOE agents, together with over 200 Greek guerrillas from both ELAS and EDES groups, blow up the Gorgopotamos railway bridge, in one of the war's biggest sabotage acts.26 Hostilities erupt between the American and Australian soldiers in Brisbane. Fighting breaks out which results in fatalities, it is dubbed the Battle of Brisbane.27 At Toulon, the French navy scuttles its ships (most notably Dunkerque and Strasbourg) and submarines to keep them out of German hands; the French have declined another option – to join the Allied fleets in North African waters.29 The Allied offensive in Tunisia meets with only minimum success.30 The naval Battle of Tassafaronga (off Guadalcanal); this is a night action in which Japanese naval forces sink one American cruiser and damage three others.30 Publication of the Beveridge Report in the United Kingdom on the post-war nature of social welfare30 The Free French liberate the island of Réunion on the Indian Ocean from the Vichy regime.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Torch" title="Operation Torch">Operation Torch</a>, the Allied invasion of Vichy-controlled <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Morocco" title="Morocco">Morocco</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Algeria" title="Algeria">Algeria</a>, begins.<dd>8-16: French resistance coup in Algiers, consisting of about 400 fighters neutralise the Vichyist XIXth Army Corps and the Vichyist generals (Juin, Darlan, etc.), contributing significantly to the immediate success of the operation.</dd><dd>8: The United States Combat Command "B" of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/1st_Armored_Division_(United_States)" title="1st Armored Division (United States)">1st Armored Division</a> lands east and west of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oran" title="Oran">Oran</a> as part of Operation Torch.</dd><dd>10: In violation of a 1940 armistice, Germany invades <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vichy_France" title="Vichy France">Vichy France</a>; they are responding to the fact that French Admiral <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fran%C3%A7ois_Darlan" title="François Darlan">François Darlan</a> has signed an armistice with the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Allies_of_World_War_II" title="Allies of World War II">Allies</a> in North Africa.</dd><dd>10: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oran" title="Oran">Oran</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Algeria" title="Algeria">Algeria</a> falls to US troops; 17 French ships are sunk at Oran, causing a rift between the French and the Allies. There are more Allied landings near the Tunisian border.</dd><dd>10: Montgomery begins a major British offensive beginning at Sollum on the Libya/Egypt border. But it is, perhaps, the end of the beginning."</dd><dd>11: Convoys reach Malta from Alexandria; an official announcement proclaims that the island is "relieved of its siege".</dd><dd>12: <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Guadalcanal" title="Battle of Guadalcanal">Battle of Guadalcanal</a> - A climactic naval battle near <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Guadalcanal_(Pacific_Ocean_island)" title="Guadalcanal (Pacific Ocean island)">Guadalcanal</a> starts between Japanese and American naval forces.</dd><dd>12: The Red Army makes an attempt to relieve Stalingrad at Kotelnikov.</dd><dd>13: <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_Eighth_Army" title="British Eighth Army">British Eighth Army</a> recaptures <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tobruk" title="Tobruk">Tobruk</a>.</dd><dd>13: Battle of Guadalcanal: aviators from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/USS_Enterprise_(CV-6)" title="USS Enterprise (CV-6)">USS <i>Enterprise</i></a> sink the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_battleship_Hiei" title="Japanese battleship Hiei">Japanese battleship <i>Hiei</i></a>. Notably, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/USS_Juneau_(CL-52)" title="USS Juneau (CL-52)">USS <i>Juneau</i></a> is sunk with much of its crew, including the five <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sullivan_brothers" title="Sullivan brothers">Sullivan brothers</a>.</dd><dd>14: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/USS_Washington_(BB-56)" title="USS Washington (BB-56)">USS <i>Washington</i></a> attacks the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_battleship_Kirishima" title="Japanese battleship Kirishima">Japanese battleship <i>Kirishima</i></a>; the Japanese ship would capsize at 03:25 on the morning of 15 November.</dd><dd>15: The naval battle of Guadalcanal ends. Although the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">United States Navy</a> suffers heavy losses, it still retains control of the sea around <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Guadalcanal_(Pacific_Ocean_island)" title="Guadalcanal (Pacific Ocean island)">Guadalcanal</a>.</dd><dd>15: The British move westward in Tunisia.</dd><dd>16: <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_Eighth_Army" title="British Eighth Army">British Eighth Army</a> recaptures <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Derna,_Libya" title="Derna, Libya">Derna</a>.</dd><dd>17: Japanese send reinforcements into New Guinea; Americans are stymied at Buna.</dd><dd>18: Heavy British RAF raid on Berlin with few losses.</dd><dd>19: At <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stalingrad" title="Stalingrad">Stalingrad</a> the Soviet Union forces under General <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Georgy_Zhukov" title="Georgy Zhukov">Georgy Zhukov</a> launch <b><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Uranus" title="Operation Uranus">Operation Uranus</a></b> aimed at encircling the Germans in the city and thus turning the tide of battle in the USSR's favor.</dd><dd>20: The Allies take <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Benghazi" title="Benghazi">Benghazi</a>, Libya; the Afrika Corps continues the retreat westward.</dd><dd>21: The Red Army attempt at encirclement of Stalingrad continues with obvious success.</dd><dd>21: American army moves to shove Japanese off the extreme western end of Guadalcanal.</dd><dd>22: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Stalingrad" title="Battle of Stalingrad">Battle of Stalingrad</a>: The situation for the German attackers of <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stalingrad" title="Stalingrad">Stalingrad</a> seems desperate during the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet</a> counter-attack; General <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Friedrich_Paulus" title="Friedrich Paulus">Friedrich Paulus</a> sends <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Adolf_Hitler" title="Adolf Hitler">Adolf Hitler</a> a telegram saying that the German 6th Army is surrounded.</dd><dd>22: Red Army troops complete the encirclement of the Germans at Kalach, west of Stalingrad.</dd><dd>23: "Der Kessel"-- the Cauldron, a description of the heavy fighting at Stalingrad; Hitler orders General Paulus not to retreat, at any cost.</dd><dd>25: The encirclement of Stalingrad continues to stabilise. Hitler reiterates his demand of Paulus not to surrender.</dd><dd>25: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Harling" title="Operation Harling">Operation Harling</a>: a team of British <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Special_Operations_Executive" title="Special Operations Executive">SOE</a> agents, together with over 200 Greek guerrillas from both <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greek_People%27s_Liberation_Army" title="Greek People's Liberation Army">ELAS</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/EDES" title="EDES">EDES</a> groups, blow up the Gorgopotamos railway bridge, in one of the war's biggest sabotage acts.</dd><dd>26: Hostilities erupt between the American and Australian soldiers in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brisbane" title="Brisbane">Brisbane</a>. Fighting breaks out which results in fatalities, it is dubbed the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Brisbane" title="Battle of Brisbane">Battle of Brisbane</a>.</dd><dd>27: At <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Toulon" title="Toulon">Toulon</a>, the French navy scuttles its ships (most notably <i>Dunkerque</i> and <i>Strasbourg</i>) and submarines to keep them out of German hands; the French have declined another option – to join the Allied fleets in North African waters.</dd><dd>29: The Allied offensive in Tunisia meets with only minimum success.</dd><dd>30: The naval <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Tassafaronga" title="Battle of Tassafaronga">Battle of Tassafaronga</a> (off Guadalcanal); this is a night action in which Japanese naval forces sink one American cruiser and damage three others.</dd><dd>30: Publication of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beveridge_Report" title="Beveridge Report">Beveridge Report</a> in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> on the post-war nature of <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Social_welfare" title="Social welfare">social welfare</a></dd><dd>30: The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Free_France" title="Free France">Free French</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_R%C3%A9union" title="Battle of Réunion">liberate</a> the island of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/R%C3%A9union" title="Réunion">Réunion</a> on the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Indian_Ocean" title="Indian Ocean">Indian Ocean</a> from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vichy_France" title="Vichy France">the Vichy regime</a>.</dd></dd>

November 11, 1940
-British naval forces launch attack against Italian navy at Taranto. Swordfish bombers from HMS Illustrious damage three battleships, two cruisers and multiple auxiliary craft.  The event secures British supply lines in the Mediterranean. The British success will be studied by Japanese military already preparing for an attack on Pearl Harbor.
-<dd> British naval forces launch attack against Italian navy at <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Taranto" title="Battle of Taranto">Taranto</a>. The event secures British supply lines in the Mediterranean. The British success will be studied by Japanese military already preparing for an <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Attack_on_Pearl_Harbor" title="Attack on Pearl Harbor">attack on Pearl Harbor</a>.</dd>

November 26, 1941
-A Japanese attack fleet of 33 warships and auxiliary craft, including six aircraft carriers, sails from northern Japan for the Hawaiian Islands. The Hull note ultimatum is delivered to Japan by the United States. After his brief dash into Egypt, Rommel retreats to Bardia for refuelling; it is during this brief withdrawal that Tobruk is temporarily relieved when the 8th Army meets with the besieged.

November 28, 1941

November 28, 1943
-The Tehran Conference .  US President Franklin D. Roosevelt, British Prime Minister Winston Churchill and Soviet Leader Joseph Stalin meet in Tehran to discuss war strategy; (on 30 November they establish an agreement concerning a planned June 1944 invasion of Europe codenamed Operation Overlord). Stalin at last has the promise he has been waiting for.
-<dd> The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tehran_Conference" title="Tehran Conference">Tehran Conference</a> . Roosevelt</a>, British Prime Minister <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Winston_Churchill" title="Winston Churchill">Winston Churchill</a> and Soviet Leader <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_Stalin" title="Joseph Stalin">Joseph Stalin</a> meet in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tehran" title="Tehran">Tehran</a> to discuss war strategy; (on 30 November they establish an agreement concerning a planned June 1944 invasion of Europe codenamed <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Overlord" title="Operation Overlord">Operation Overlord</a>). Stalin at last has the promise he has been waiting for.</dd>

November 29, 1945
-The prohibition against marriage between GIs and Austrian women was rescinded on November 29. Later it would be rescinded for German women too. Black soldiers serving in the army were not allowed to marry white women, (in the case that they remained in the army) so they were restricted until 1948 when the prohibition against interracial marriages was removed.
-<dd> The prohibition against marriage between GIs and Austrian women was rescinded on November 29. Later it would be rescinded for German women too. Black soldiers serving in the army were not allowed to marry white women, (in the case that they remained in the army) so they were restricted until 1948 when the prohibition against interracial marriages was removed.</dd>
December 1, 1939
-Russia continues its war against Finland; Helsinki is bombed. In the first two weeks of the month, the Finns retreat to the Mannerheim line, an outmoded defensive line just inside the southern border with Russia.

December 1, 1940
-[1-8] Greek forces continue to drive the Italian armies back, capturing the cities of Pogradec, Sarandë, and Gjirokastër.
-<dd> Greek forces continue to drive the Italian armies back, capturing the cities of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pogradec" title="Pogradec">Pogradec</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sarand%C3%AB" title="Sarandë">Sarandë</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gjirokast%C3%ABr" title="Gjirokastër">Gjirokastër</a>.</dd>
December 1, 1940
-Bombing raids are exchanged throughout the month between Germany and Britain. First German bombs, then Britain's.
-<dd> Bombing raids are exchanged throughout the month between Germany and Britain. First German bombs, then Britain's.</dd>
December 1, 1940
-Joseph P. Kennedy, the US Ambassador to the United Kingdom is asked to resign by President Roosevelt after he gives a newspaper interview expressing the view that "Democracy is finished in England".
-<dd> <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_P._Kennedy" title="Joseph P. Kennedy">Joseph P. Kennedy</a>, the US Ambassador to the United Kingdom is asked to resign by President Roosevelt after he gives a newspaper interview expressing the view that "Democracy is finished in England".</dd>
December 1, 1941
-Malta marks its 1,000th bombing raid. Fiorello H. La Guardia publishes Administrative Order 9 creating the Civil Air Patrol for U.S Coastal Patrol and naming its national commander Major General John F. Curry. Approximately 20,000 Stanisławów Jews ordered into the Ghetto area, and non-Jews ordered out. SS officer Karl Jaeger reports "Lithuania clean of Jews" with some exceptions.
-<dd> Malta marks its 1,000th bombing raid. <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fiorello_H._La_Guardia" title="Fiorello H. La Guardia">Fiorello H. La Guardia</a> publishes <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Administrative_Order_9" title="s:Administrative Order 9">Administrative Order 9</a> creating the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Civil_Air_Patrol" title="Civil Air Patrol">Civil Air Patrol</a> for U.S Coastal Patrol and naming its national commander Major General <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_F._Curry" title="John F. Curry">John F. Curry</a>. Approximately 20,000 Stanisławów Jews ordered into <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stanis%C5%82aw%C3%B3w_Ghetto" title="Stanisławów Ghetto">the Ghetto area</a>, and non-Jews ordered out. SS officer <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Karl_J%C3%A4ger" title="Karl Jäger">Karl Jaeger</a> reports "Lithuania clean of Jews" with some exceptions.</dd>
December 1, 1942
-Gasoline rationing begins in the United States.1 The US cruiser Northampton is sunk as Japanese destroyers attempt to come down "the Slot" to Guadalcanal.2 Heavy fighting in Tunisia, as German forces are pushed into the final North African corner.2 Below the bleachers of Stagg Field at the University of Chicago, a team led by Enrico Fermi initiate the first nuclear chain reaction. A coded message, "The Italian navigator has landed in the new world" is sent to President Roosevelt.4 The first US bombing of mainland Italy --Naples.4 Carlson's patrol ends.6 RAF bombs Eindhoven, the Netherlands.7 On the anniversary of the Pearl Harbor attack, USS New Jersey, America's largest battleship is launched (commissioned five months later).7-12 British commandos conduct Operation Frankton a raid on shipping in Bordeaux harbour.9 The Marines turn over Guadalcanal to the American army.12 Rommel abandons El Agheila and retreats to Tripoli; the final stand will be at the Mareth line in southern Tunisia.12-23 In a large operation named "Operation Winter Storm", the Germans attempt to break through to forces trapped in Stalingrad.13 The Luftwaffe flies in meagre supplies to the beleaguered Stalingrad troops.15 American and Australian troops finally push Japanese out of Buna, New Guinea.15 Allies clash with Japanese troops in the Battle of the Gifu.22 The Germans begin a retreat from the Caucasus.22 The battle for "Longstop Hill" begins; a key position outside Tunis, the Germans eventually take it and hold it until April.22 The remainder of the United States 1st Armored Division arrived at North Africa for Operation Husky.23 Japanese air force planes begin bombing of Calcutta.24 French Admiral Darlan, the former Vichy leader who had switched over to the Allies following the Torch landings, is assassinated in Algiers.24 The United States reorganizes its Combat Arms Regiments with their Organic Battalions into Separate Groups and Battalions.25 American bombers hit Rabaul.26 Heavy fighting continues on Guadalcanal, now focused on Mount Austen in the west.28 The governor of pro-Vichy French Somaliland surrenders to invading British and Free French forces.31 In the Battle of the Barents Sea, the British win a strategic victory, leading Hitler to largely abandon the use of surface raiders in favor of U-boats.
-<dd> Gasoline rationing begins in the United States.<dd>1: The US cruiser <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/USS_Northampton_(CA-26)" title="USS Northampton (CA-26)"><i>Northampton</i></a> is sunk as Japanese destroyers attempt to come down "the Slot" to Guadalcanal.</dd><dd>2: Heavy fighting in Tunisia, as German forces are pushed into the final North African corner.</dd><dd>2: Below the bleachers of Stagg Field at the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/University_of_Chicago" title="University of Chicago">University of Chicago</a>, a team led by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Enrico_Fermi" title="Enrico Fermi">Enrico Fermi</a> initiate the first <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nuclear_chain_reaction" title="Nuclear chain reaction">nuclear chain reaction</a>. A coded message, "The Italian navigator has landed in the new world" is sent to President Roosevelt.</dd><dd>4: The first US bombing of mainland Italy --Naples.</dd><dd>4: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Carlson%27s_patrol" title="Carlson's patrol">Carlson's patrol</a> ends.</dd><dd>6: RAF bombs <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eindhoven" title="Eindhoven">Eindhoven</a>, the Netherlands.</dd><dd>7: On the anniversary of the Pearl Harbor attack, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/USS_New_Jersey_(BB-62)" title="USS New Jersey (BB-62)">USS <i>New Jersey</i></a>, America's largest battleship is launched (commissioned five months later).</dd><dd>7-12: British commandos conduct <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Frankton" title="Operation Frankton">Operation Frankton</a> a raid on shipping in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bordeaux" title="Bordeaux">Bordeaux</a> harbour.</dd><dd>9: The Marines turn over Guadalcanal to the American army.</dd><dd>12: Rommel abandons El Agheila and retreats to Tripoli; the final stand will be at the Mareth line in southern Tunisia.</dd><dd>12-23: In a large operation named "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Winter_Storm" title="Operation Winter Storm">Operation Winter Storm</a>", the Germans attempt to break through to forces trapped in Stalingrad.</dd><dd>13: The Luftwaffe flies in meagre supplies to the beleaguered Stalingrad troops.</dd><dd>15: American and Australian troops finally push Japanese out of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Buna,_Papua_New_Guinea" title="Buna, Papua New Guinea">Buna</a>, New Guinea.</dd><dd>15: Allies clash with Japanese troops in the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Mount_Austen,_the_Galloping_Horse,_and_the_Sea_Horse" title="Battle of Mount Austen, the Galloping Horse, and the Sea Horse">Battle of the Gifu</a>.</dd><dd>22: The Germans begin a retreat from the Caucasus.</dd><dd>22: The battle for "Longstop Hill" begins; a key position outside Tunis, the Germans eventually take it and hold it until April.</dd><dd>22: The remainder of the United States <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/1st_Armored_Division_(United_States)" title="1st Armored Division (United States)">1st Armored Division</a> arrived at North Africa for <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Husky" title="Operation Husky">Operation Husky</a>.</dd><dd>23: Japanese air force planes begin bombing of Calcutta.</dd><dd>24: French <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fran%C3%A7ois_Darlan" title="François Darlan">Admiral Darlan</a>, the former <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vichy_France" title="Vichy France">Vichy</a> leader who had switched over to the Allies following the Torch landings, is assassinated in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Algiers" title="Algiers">Algiers</a>.</dd><dd>24: The United States reorganizes its Combat Arms Regiments with their Organic Battalions into Separate Groups and Battalions.</dd><dd>25: American bombers hit <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rabaul" title="Rabaul">Rabaul</a>.</dd><dd>26: Heavy fighting continues on Guadalcanal, now focused on Mount Austen in the west.</dd><dd>28: The governor of pro-Vichy <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_Somaliland" title="French Somaliland">French Somaliland</a> surrenders to <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_invasion_of_French_Somaliland" title="British invasion of French Somaliland">invading British and Free French forces</a>.</dd><dd>31: In the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_the_Barents_Sea" title="Battle of the Barents Sea">Battle of the Barents Sea</a>, the British win a strategic victory, leading Hitler to largely abandon the use of surface raiders in favor of U-boats.</dd></dd>

December 2, 1939
-The Red Army takes Petsamo.
-<dd> The Red Army takes <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pechengsky_District" title="Pechengsky District">Petsamo</a>.</dd>
December 2, 1941
-Prime Minister Tojo rejects "peace feelers" from the US. A German combat engineer patrol reaches the town of Khimki while scouting for a hole in the Russian defense perimeter around Moscow. It is the closest advance the Germans make to the Russian capital.
-<dd> Prime Minister Tojo rejects "peace feelers" from the US. A German combat engineer patrol reaches the town of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Khimki" title="Khimki">Khimki</a> while scouting for a hole in the Russian defense perimeter around Moscow. It is the closest advance the Germans make to the Russian capital.</dd>
December 2, 1942
-Heavy fighting in Tunisia, as German forces are pushed into the final North African corner.
-<dd> Heavy fighting in Tunisia, as German forces are pushed into the final North African corner.</dd>
December 2, 1942
-Below the bleachers of Stagg Field at the University of Chicago, a team led by Enrico Fermi initiate the first nuclear chain reaction. A coded message, "The Italian navigator has landed in the new world" is sent to President Roosevelt.
-<dd> Below the bleachers of Stagg Field at the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/University_of_Chicago" title="University of Chicago">University of Chicago</a>, a team led by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Enrico_Fermi" title="Enrico Fermi">Enrico Fermi</a> initiate the first <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nuclear_chain_reaction" title="Nuclear chain reaction">nuclear chain reaction</a>. A coded message, "The Italian navigator has landed in the new world" is sent to President Roosevelt.</dd>
December 2, 1943
-The Germans conduct a highly successful Air Raid on Bari, Italy. One of the German bombs hits an Allied cargo ship carrying mustard gas, releasing the chemical which killed 83 Allied soldiers. Over 1000 other soldiers died in the raid.
-<dd> The Germans conduct a highly successful <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Air_Raid_on_Bari" title="Air Raid on Bari">Air Raid on Bari</a>, Italy. One of the German bombs hits an Allied cargo ship carrying <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mustard_gas" title="Mustard gas">mustard gas</a>, releasing the chemical which killed 83 Allied soldiers. Over 1000 other soldiers died in the raid.</dd>
December 3, 1941
-Conscription in the United Kingdom now includes all men between 18 and 50. Women will not be neglected since they will serve in fire brigades and in women's auxiliary groups.
-<dd> Conscription in the United Kingdom now includes all men between 18 and 50. Women will not be neglected since they will serve in fire brigades and in women's auxiliary groups.</dd>
December 3, 1941
-General strike begins among native mine-workers in the Belgian Congo.

December 3, 1941
-Vilna Ghetto 'Criminal Aktion' begins, continued the next day. 157 Jews are killed at Ponary.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vilna_Ghetto" title="Vilna Ghetto">Vilna Ghetto</a> 'Criminal Aktion' begins, continued the next day. 157 Jews are killed at Ponary.</dd>
December 3, 1943
-Edward R. Murrow delivers his classic "Orchestrated Hell" broadcast over CBS Radio describing a Royal Air Force nighttime bombing raid on Berlin.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_R._Murrow" title="Edward R. Murrow">Edward R. Murrow</a> delivers his classic "Orchestrated Hell" broadcast over <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/CBS" title="CBS">CBS</a> Radio describing a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Royal_Air_Force" title="Royal Air Force">Royal Air Force</a> nighttime bombing raid on <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Berlin" title="Berlin">Berlin</a>.</dd>
December 3, 1944
-The British army and the police shot unarmed protestors in Athens; the crowd carried Greek, American, British and Soviet flags, and chanted "Viva Churchill, Viva Roosevelt, Viva Stalin’"
-<dd>The British army and the police shot unarmed protestors in Athens; the crowd carried Greek, American, British and Soviet flags, and chanted: "Viva Churchill, Viva Roosevelt, Viva Stalin’"</dd>
December 3, 1944
-The Dekemvriana ("December events") begin in the Greek capital, Athens, between members of the leftist National Liberation Front and government forces, backed by the British. The clashes are limited to Athens, however, and the rest of the country remains relatively tranquil. The British Home Guard is stood down.
-<dd> The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dekemvriana" title="Dekemvriana">Dekemvriana</a> ("December events") begin in the Greek capital, Athens, between members of the leftist National Liberation Front and government forces, backed by the British. The clashes are limited to Athens, however, and the rest of the country remains relatively tranquil. The <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_Home_Guard" title="British Home Guard">British Home Guard</a> is stood down.</dd>

-The temperature on the Moscow front falls to −31 °F (−37 °C). German attacks are failing.

December 5, 1939
-The Russian invaders start heavy attacks on the Mannerheim line. The Battles of Kollaa and Suomussalmi begin.
-<dd> The Russian invaders start heavy attacks on the Mannerheim line. December 5, 1940
-The RAF bombs Düsseldorf and Turin.
-<dd> The RAF bombs Düsseldorf and Turin.</dd>
December 5, 1941
-Germans call off the attack on Moscow, now 11 miles away; the USSR counter-attacks during a heavy blizzard.
-<dd> Germans call off the attack on Moscow, now 11 miles away; the USSR counter-attacks during a heavy blizzard.</dd>
December 5, 1944
-The Allies are now in control of Ravenna, Italy.
-<dd> The Allies are now in control of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ravenna" title="Ravenna">Ravenna</a>, Italy.</dd>
December 6, 1940
-[6-9] British and Indian troops of the Western Desert Force launch Operation Compass, an offensive against Italian forces in Egypt.  The Italians have seven infantry divisions and the Maletti Group in fortified defensive positions.  Initial attacks are launched against the five Italian camps around and south of Sidi Barrani.  The camps are overrun, Italian General Pietro Maletti is killed, and the Maletti Group, the 1st Libyan Division, the 2nd Libyan Division, and the 4th Blackshirt Division are all but destroyed.  The remaining Italian units in Egypt are forced to withdraw towards Libya.
-<dd> British and Indian troops of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Western_Desert_Force" title="Western Desert Force">Western Desert Force</a> launch <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Compass" title="Operation Compass">Operation Compass</a>, an offensive against Italian forces in Egypt.  The Italians have seven infantry divisions and the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maletti_Group" title="Maletti Group">Maletti Group</a> in fortified defensive positions.  Initial attacks are launched against the five Italian camps around and south of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sidi_Barrani" title="Sidi Barrani">Sidi Barrani</a>.  The camps are overrun, Italian General <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pietro_Maletti" title="Pietro Maletti">Pietro Maletti</a> is killed, and the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maletti_Group" title="Maletti Group">Maletti Group</a>, the 1st Libyan Division, the 2nd Libyan Division, and the 4th Blackshirt Division are all but destroyed.  The remaining Italian units in Egypt are forced to withdraw towards Libya.</dd>
December 6, 1941
-The United Kingdom declares war on Finland. Vilna Ghetto Gestapo Workers Aktion – 800 Jews and 10 Poles shot at the Ponary massacre death site. Temperatures are minus 23 degrees Celsius.
-<dd> The United Kingdom declares war on Finland. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vilna_Ghetto" title="Vilna Ghetto">Vilna Ghetto</a> Gestapo Workers Aktion – 800 Jews and 10 Poles shot at the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ponary_massacre" title="Ponary massacre">Ponary massacre</a> death site. Temperatures are minus 23 degrees Celsius.</dd>

-RAF bombs Eindhoven, the Netherlands.
