December 7, 1939
-Italy again declares its neutrality. Norway, Sweden, and Denmark also proclaim their neutrality in the Russo-Finnish quarrel.
-<dd> Italy again declares its neutrality. Norway, Sweden, and Denmark also proclaim their neutrality in the Russo-Finnish quarrel.</dd>
December 7, 1941
-(December 8, Asian time zones) Japan launches an attack on Pearl Harbor, declares war on the United States and the United Kingdom and invades Thailand and British Malaya and launches aerial attacks against Guam, Hong Kong, the Philippines, Shanghai, Singapore and Wake Island. Canada declares war on Japan. Australia declares war on Japan. Adolf Hitler signs the German "Night and Fog decree" dictating the elimination of anti-Nazi resistance activities in Western Europe.
-<dd> (December 8, Asian time zones) Japan launches an attack on <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pearl_Harbor" title="Pearl Harbor">Pearl Harbor</a>, declares war on the United States and the United Kingdom and invades <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_Malaya" title="British Malaya">British Malaya</a> and launches aerial attacks against <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Guam" title="Guam">Guam</a>, Hong Kong, the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>, Shanghai, Singapore and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wake_Island" title="Wake Island">Wake Island</a>. Canada declares war on Japan. Australia declares war on Japan. Adolf Hitler signs the German <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nacht_und_Nebel" title="Nacht und Nebel">"Night and Fog</a> decree" dictating the elimination of anti-Nazi resistance activities in Western Europe.</dd>
December 7, 1942
-On the anniversary of the Pearl Harbor attack, USS New Jersey, America's largest battleship is launched (commissioned five months later).
-<dd> On the anniversary of the Pearl Harbor attack, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/USS_New_Jersey_(BB-62)" title="USS New Jersey (BB-62)">USS <i>New Jersey</i></a>, America's largest battleship is launched (commissioned five months later).</dd>
December 7, 1942
-[7-12] British commandos conduct Operation Frankton a raid on shipping in Bordeaux harbour.
-<dd> British commandos conduct <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Frankton" title="Operation Frankton">Operation Frankton</a> a raid on shipping in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bordeaux" title="Bordeaux">Bordeaux</a> harbour.</dd>
December 8, 1940
-[1-8] Greek forces continue to drive the Italian armies back, capturing the cities of Pogradec, Sarandë, and Gjirokastër.
-<dd> Greek forces continue to drive the Italian armies back, capturing the cities of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pogradec" title="Pogradec">Pogradec</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sarand%C3%AB" title="Sarandë">Sarandë</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gjirokast%C3%ABr" title="Gjirokastër">Gjirokastër</a>.</dd>
December 8, 1940
-Francisco Franco rules out Spanish entry into the war; the immediate result is that Hitler is forced to cancel an attack on Gibraltar.
-<dd> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Francisco_Franco" title="Francisco Franco">Francisco Franco</a> rules out Spanish entry into the war; the immediate result is that Hitler is forced to cancel an attack on Gibraltar.</dd>
December 8, 1941
-The United States, the United Kingdom, the Netherlands and New Zealand declare war on Japan. Japanese forces take the Gilbert Islands (which include Tarawa). Clark Field in the Philippines is bombed, and many American aircraft are destroyed on the ground. Japanese troops attack Thailand in the Battle of Prachuab Khirikhan. The Battle of Hong Kong begins The Malayan Campaign begins. Kamenka, Krasnaya Polyana, and Kriukovo, are liberated by the Workers' and Peasants' Red Army. The Germans are never again within artillery range of Moscow.
-<dd> The United States, the United Kingdom, the Netherlands and New Zealand declare war on Japan. Japanese forces take the Gilbert Islands (which include Tarawa). <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Clark_Air_Base" title="Clark Air Base">Clark Field</a> in the Philippines is bombed, and many American aircraft are destroyed on the ground. Japanese troops attack Thailand in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Prachuab_Khirikhan" title="Battle of Prachuab Khirikhan">Battle of Prachuab Khirikhan</a>. The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Battle_of_Hong_Kong" title="Battle of Hong Kong">Battle of Hong Kong</a> begins: The <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malayan_Campaign" title="Malayan Campaign">Malayan Campaign</a> begins. Kamenka, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lobnya" title="Lobnya">Krasnaya Polyana</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kryukovo_District" title="Kryukovo District">Kriukovo</a>, are liberated by the <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Workers%27_and_Peasants%27_Red_Army" title="Workers' and Peasants' Red Army">Workers' and Peasants' Red Army</a>. The Germans are never again within artillery range of <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moscow,_Russia" title="Moscow, Russia">Moscow</a>.</dd>
December 8, 1944
-The softening-up bombardment of Iwo Jima begins.
-<dd> The softening-up bombardment of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Iwo_Jima" title="Iwo Jima">Iwo Jima</a> begins.</dd>
December 9, 1940
-[6-9] British and Indian troops of the Western Desert Force launch Operation Compass, an offensive against Italian forces in Egypt.  The Italians have seven infantry divisions and the Maletti Group in fortified defensive positions.  Initial attacks are launched against the five Italian camps around and south of Sidi Barrani.  The camps are overrun, Italian General Pietro Maletti is killed, and the Maletti Group, the 1st Libyan Division, the 2nd Libyan Division, and the 4th Blackshirt Division are all but destroyed.  The remaining Italian units in Egypt are forced to withdraw towards Libya.
-<dd> British and Indian troops of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Western_Desert_Force" title="Western Desert Force">Western Desert Force</a> launch <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Operation_Compass" title="Operation Compass">Operation Compass</a>, an offensive against Italian forces in Egypt.  The Italians have seven infantry divisions and the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maletti_Group" title="Maletti Group">Maletti Group</a> in fortified defensive positions.  Initial attacks are launched against the five Italian camps around and south of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sidi_Barrani" title="Sidi Barrani">Sidi Barrani</a>.  The camps are overrun, Italian General <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pietro_Maletti" title="Pietro Maletti">Pietro Maletti</a> is killed, and the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maletti_Group" title="Maletti Group">Maletti Group</a>, the 1st Libyan Division, the 2nd Libyan Division, and the 4th Blackshirt Division are all but destroyed.  The remaining Italian units in Egypt are forced to withdraw towards Libya.</dd>
December 9, 1941
-China officially declares war on Japan, although a de facto state of war has existed between the two countries since the Marco Polo Bridge Incident of July 7, 1937. China also declares war on Germany and Italy. Australia officially declares war on Japan. South Africa declares war on Japan, regarded as if at war from eight December 1941.
-<dd> <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Republic_of_China" title="The Republic of China">China</a> officially declares war on Japan, although a <i>de facto</i> state of war has existed between the two countries since the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Marco_Polo_Bridge_Incident" title="Marco Polo Bridge Incident">Marco Polo Bridge Incident</a> of July 7, 1937. China also declares war on Germany and Italy. Australia officially declares war on Japan. South Africa declares war on Japan, regarded as if at war from eight December 1941.</dd>
December 9, 1941
-Striking miners of the Union Minière at Elizabethville in the Belgian Congo are fired on by Belgian colonial forces during negotiations, killing an estimated 70 people.

December 24, 1941
-In the Philippines, American forces retreat into Bataan Peninsula. Japanese bomb Rangoon. All Jewish ghettos in Nazi-occupied Europe are required to gather all fur coats or other furs from the Jews. On Christmas Eve the Free French liberate Saint Pierre and Miquelon from Vichy France.
-<dd> In the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>, American forces retreat into <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bataan_Peninsula" title="Bataan Peninsula">Bataan Peninsula</a>. All Jewish <a class="mw-redirect" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ghettos_in_Nazi-occupied_Europe" title="Ghettos in Nazi-occupied Europe">ghettos in Nazi-occupied Europe</a> are required to gather all fur coats or other furs from the Jews. On Christmas Eve the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Free_France" title="Free France">Free French</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/History_of_Saint_Pierre_and_Miquelon#World_War_II" title="History of Saint Pierre and Miquelon">liberate</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saint_Pierre_and_Miquelon" title="Saint Pierre and Miquelon">Saint Pierre and Miquelon</a> from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vichy_France" title="Vichy France">Vichy France</a>.</dd>

-The siege of Bastogne is broken by Patton's Third Army tanks, and with it the Ardennes offensive collapses into failure. Racial tensions within the US military boil over into the Agana race riot on Guam.
